dhṛtim apahartuṃ sakhi me
dūtīva hareḥ śaran militā  RUnm 
pūrṇasudhāṃśur yathā
rākāsudhāṃśur abhavan na tamāṃsi hartuṃ
vṛndāṭavījaṭharagāny adhunāpi śaktaḥ 
rākāsudhāṃśumukhi tāni tavonnatāni
hṛtkandarāstaracarāṇi kathaṃ jahāra  RUnm 
gandhavāho
yathā śrīgītagovinde 
manobhavānandanacandanānila
prasīda re dakṣiṇa muñca vāmatām 
kṣaṇaṃ jagatprāṇa nidāya mādhavaṃ
puro mama prāṇaharo bhaviṣyasi  RUnm 
khagāḥ yathā
mānena sārdhaṃ paśupālasubhruvāṃ
marālamālā calitā ghanāgame 
kadambakuñje vijihīrṣayā samaṃ
samāgatā nāgari cātakāvalī  RUnm 
ādiśabdāt sakhīsneha ātmany uddīpano varaḥ  RUnm 
yathā
harim avekṣya puro gurto bhiyā
muhur abhūn mukulannavavibhramā 
lalitayā vivṛte nijasauhṛde
caladṛgañcalam ādhita rādhikā  RUnm 
iti śrīśrīujjvalanīlamaṇau
uddīpanavibhāvabhedaprakaraṇam 
Chapter 
atha anubhāvaprakaraṇam
anubhāvās tv alaṅkārās tathaivodbhāsvarābhidhāḥ 
vācikāś ceti vidvadbhis tridhāmī parikīrtitāḥ  RUnm 
tatra alaṅkārāḥ
yauvane sattvajās tāsām alaṅkārās tu viṃśatiḥ 
udayanty adbhutāḥ kānte sarvathābhiniveśataḥ  RUnm 
bhāvo hāvaś ca helā ca proktās tatra trayo'ṅgajāḥ  RUnm 
śobhā kāntiś ca dīptiś ca mādhuryaṃ ca pragalbhatā 
audāryaṃ dhairym ity ete saptaiva syur ayatnajāḥ  RUnm 
līlā vilāso vicchittir vibhramaḥ kilakiñcitam 
moṭṭāyitaṃ kuṭṭamitaṃ bibboko lalitaṃ tathā 
vikṛtaṃ ceti vijñeyā daśa tāsāṃ svabhāvajāḥ  RUnm 
tatra bhāvaḥ
prādurbhāvaṃ vrajaty eva ratyākhye bhāva ujjvale 
nirvikārātmake citte bhāvaḥ prathamavikriyā  RUnm 
tathā hy uktaṃ rasasudhākare 
cittasyāvikṛtiḥ sattvaṃ vikṛteḥ kāraṇe sati 
tatrādyā vikriyā bhāvo bījasyādivikāravat  RUnm 
yathā
pitur goṣṭhe sphīte kusumini purā khāṇḍavavane
na te dṛṣṭvā saaṅkrandanam api manaḥ spandanam agāt 
puro vṛndāraṇye viharati mukunde sakhi mudā
kim āndolād akṣṇaḥ śrutikumudam indīvaram abhūt  RUnm 
atha hāvaḥ
grīvārecakasaṃyukto bhrūnetrādivikāśakṛt 
bhāvād īṣatprakāśo yaḥ sa hāva iti kathyate  RUnm 
yathā
sācistambhitakaṇṭhi kuḍmalavatīṃ netrālir abhyeti te
ghūrṇan karṇalatāṃ manāg vikasitā bhrūvallarī nṛtyati 
atra prādurabhūt taṭe sumanasām ullāsakas tvatpuro
gaurāṅgi prathamaṃ vanapriayabandhuḥ sphuṭaṃ mādhavaḥ  RUnm 
atha helā
hāva eva bhaved dhelā vyaktaśṛṅgārasūcakaḥ  RUnm 
yathā
śrute veṇau vakṣaḥ sphurtiakucam ādhmātam api te
tirovikṣiptākṣaṃ pulakitakapolaṃ ca vadanam 
skhalatkāñci svedārgalitasicayaṃ cāpi jaghanaṃ
pramādaṃ mā kārṣīḥ sakhi carati savye gurujanaḥ  RUnm 
atha ayatnajāḥ 
tatra śobhā
sā śobhā rūpabhogādyair yat syād aṅgavibhūṣaṇam  RUnm 
yathā
dhṛtvā raktāṅgulikiśalayair nīpaśākhāṃ viśākhā
niṣkrāmantī vratatibhavanāt prātar udghūrṇitākṣī 
veṇīm aṃsopari viluṭhatīm ardham uktāṃ vahantī
lagnā svānte mama na hi bahiḥ seyam adyāpy ayāsīt  RUnm 
atha kāntiḥ
śobhaiva kāntir ākhyātā manmathāpyāyanojjvalā  RUnm 
yathā
prakṛtimadhuramūrtir bāḍham atrāpy udañca
ttaruṇimanavalakṣmīlekhayāliṅgitāṅgī 
varamadanavihārair adya tatrāpy udārā
madayati hṛdayaṃ me rundhatī rādhikeyam  RUnm 
atha dīptiḥ
kāntir eva vayobhogadeśakālaguṇādibhiḥ 
uddīpitātivistāraṃ prāptā ced dīptir ucyate  RUnm 
yathā
nimīlannetraśrīr acaṭulapaṭīrācalamaru
nnipītasvedāmbus truṭadamalahārojjvalakucā 
nikuñje kṣiptāṅgī śaśikiraṇakirmīritataṭe
kiśorī sā tene harimanasi rādhā manasijam  RUnm 
atha mādhuryam
mādhuryaṃ nāma ceṣṭānāṃ sarvāvasthāsu cārutā  RUnm 
yathā
asavyaṃ kaṃsārer bhujaśirasi dhṛtvā pulakinaṃ
nijaśroṇyāṃ savyaṃ karam anṛjuviṣkambhitapadā 
dadhānā mūrdhānaṃ laghutaratiraḥsraṃsinam iyaṃ
babhau rāsottīrṇā muhur alasamūrtiḥ śaśimukhī  RUnm 
atha pragalbhatā
niḥśaṅkatvaṃ prayogeṣu budhair uktā pragalbhatā  RUnm 
yathā vidagdhamādhave 
prātikūlyam iva yad vivṛṇvatī
rādhikā radanakhārpaṇoddhūrā 
kelikarmaṇi gatā pravīṇatāṃ
tena tuṣṭim atulāṃ harir yayau  RUnm 
atha audāryam
audāryaṃ vinayaṃ prāhuḥ sarvāvasthāgataṃ budhāḥ  RUnm 
yathā vidagdhamādhave  
nyaviśata nayanānte kāpi sāralyaniṣṭhā
vacasi ca vinayena stotrabhaṅgī nyavātsīt 
ajani ca mayi bhūyān sambhramas tena tasyā
vyavṛṇuta hṛdi manyuṃ suṣṭhu dākṣiṇyam eva  RUnm 
yathā vā
kṛtajño'pi premojjvalamatir api sphāravinayo'
pyabhijñānāṃ cuḍāmaṇir api kṛpānīradhir api 
yad antaḥsvaccho'pi smarati na harir gokulabhuvaṃ
mamaivedaṃ janmāntaraduritadusṭadrumaphalam  RUnm 
atha dhairyam
sthirā cittonnatir yā tu tad dhairyam iti kīrtyate  RUnm 
yathā lalitamādhave 
audāsīnyadhurāparītahṛdayaḥ kāṭhinyam ālambatāṃ
kāmaṃ śyāmalasundaro mayi sakhi svairī sahasraṃ samāḥ 
kintu bhrāntibharād api kṣaṇam idaṃ tatra priyebhyaḥ priye
ceto janmani janmani praṇayitād āsyaṃ na me hāsyati  RUnm 
atha svabhāvajāḥ  tatra līlā
priyānukaraṇaṃ līlā ramyair veśakriyādibhiḥ  RUnm 
yathā viṣṇupurāṇe 
duṣṭakāliya tiṣṭhādya kṛṣṇo'ham iti cāparā 
bāhum āsphoṭya kṛṣṇasya līlāsarvasvam ādade  RUnm 
yathā vā chandomañjaryām
mṛgamadakṛtacarcā pītakauṣeyavāsā
ruciraśikhiśikhaṇḍā baddhadhammillapāśā 
anṛjunihitam aṃse vaṃśam utkvāṇayantī
kṛtamadhuripuveṣā mālinī pātu rādhā  RUnm 
atha vilāsaḥ
gatisthānāsanādīnāṃ mukhanetrādikarmaṇām 
tātkālikaṃ tu vaiśiṣṭyaṃ vilāsaḥ priyasaṅgajam  RUnm 
yathā
ruṇatsi purataḥ sphuraty aghahare kathaṃ nāsikā
śikhagrathitamauktikonnamanakaitvena smitam 
nirāsthad aciraṃ sudhākiraṇakaumudīmādhurīṃ
manāg api tavodgatā madhuradanti dantadyutiḥ  RUnm 
yathā vā
adhyāsīnam amuṃ kadambanikaṭe krīḍākuṭīrasthalī
mābhīrendrakumāram atra rabhasād ālokayantyāḥ puraḥ 
digdhā dugdhasamudramugdhalaharīlāvaṇyanisyandibhiḥ
kālindī tava dṛktaraṅgitabharais tanvaṅgi gaṅgāyate  RUnm 
atha vicchittiḥ
ākalpakalpanālpāpi vicchittiḥ kāntipoṣakṛt  RUnm 
yathā
mākandapatreṇa mukundacetaḥ
pramodinī mārutakampitena 
raktena karṇābharaṇīkṛtena
rādhāmukhāmbhoruham ullalāsa  RUnm 
yathā vā harivaṃśe
ekenāmalapatreṇa kaṇṭhasūtrāvalambinā 
rarāja barhipatreṇa mandamārutakampinā  RUnm 
sakhīyatnād iva dhṛtir maṇḍanānāṃ priyāgasi 
serṣyāvajñā varastrībhir vicchittir iti kecana  RUnm 
yathā
mudrāṃ gāḍhatarāṃ vidhāya nihite dūrīkuruṣvāṅgade
granthiṃ nyasya kaṭhoram arpitamatiḥ kaṇṭhān maṇiṃ bhraṃśaya 
mugdhe kṛṣṇabhujaṅgadṛṣṭikalayā durvārayā dūṣite
ratnālaṅkaraṇe manāg api manas tṛṣṇāṃ na puṣṇāti me  RUnm 
atha vibhramaḥ
vallabhaprāptivelāyāṃ madanāveśasambhramāt 
vibhramo hāramālyādibhūṣāsthānaviparyayaḥ  RUnm 
yathā vidagdhamādhave 
dhammillopari nīlaratnaracito hāras tvayāropito
vinyastaḥ kucakumbhayoḥ kurvalayaśreṇīkṛto garbhakaḥ 
aṅge carcitam añjanaṃ vinihitā kastūrikā netrayoḥ
kaṃsārer abhisārasambhramabharān manye jagad vismṛtam  RUnm 
yathā vā śrīdaśame 
limpantyaḥ pramṛjantyo'nyā añjantyaḥ kāś ca locane 
vyatyastavastrābharaṇāḥ kāścit kṛṣṇāntikaṃ yayuḥ  RUnm 
adhīnasyāpi sevāyāṃ kāntasyānabhinandanam 
vibhramo vāmatodrekāt syād ity ākhyāti kaścana  RUnm 
yathā
tvaṃ govinda mayāsi kiṃ nu kavarībandhārtham abhyarthitaḥ
kleśenālam abaddha eva cikurastomo mudaṃ dogdhi me 
vaktrasyāpi na mājjanaṃ kuru ghanaṃ gharmāsu me rocate
naivottaṃsaya mālatīr mama śiraḥ khedaṃ bhareṇāpsyati  RUnm 
atha kilakiñcitam
garvābhilāṣaruditasmitāsūyābhayakrudhām 
saṅkarīkaraṇaṃ harṣād ucyate kilakiñcitam  RUnm 
yathā
mayā jātollāsaṃ priyasahacarī locanapathe
balān nyaste rādhākucamukulayoḥ pāṇikamale 
udañcadbhrūbhedaṃ sapulakam avaṣṭambhi valitaṃ
smrāmy antas tasyāḥ smitaruditakāntadyuti mukham  RUnm 
yathā vā dānakelikaumudyāṃ 
antaḥsmeratayojjvalā jalakaṇavyākīrṇapakṣmāṅkurā
kiñcit pāṭalitāñcalā rasikatotsiktā puraḥ kuñcatī 
ruddhāyāḥ pathi mādhavena madhuravyābhugnatārottarā
rādhāyāḥ kilakiñcitastavakinī dṛṣṭiḥ śriyaṃ vaḥ kriyāt  RUnm 
atha moṭṭāyitam
kāntasmaraṇavārtādau hṛdi tadbhāvabhāvataḥ 
prākaṭyam abhilāṣasya moṭṭāyitam udīryate  RUnm 
yathā
na brūte klamabījam ālibhir alaṃ pṛṣṭāpi pālī yadā
cāturyeṇa tadagratas tava kathā tābhis tadā prastutā 
tāṃ pītāmbara jṛmbhamāṇavadanāmbhojā kṣaṇaṃ śṛṇvatī
bimboṣṭhī pulakari viḍambitavatī phullāṃ kadambaśriyam  RUnm 
atha kuṭṭamitam
stanādharādigrahaṇe hṛtprītāv api sambhramāt 
bahiḥ krodho vyathitavat proktaṃ kuṭṭamitaṃ budhaiḥ  RUnm 
yathā
karauddhatyaṃ hanta sthagaya kavarī me vighaṭate
dukūlaṃ ca nyañcaty aghahara tavāstāṃ vihasitam 
kim ārabdhaḥ kartuṃ tam anavasare nirdaya madāt
patāmy eṣā pīade vitara śayituṃ me kṣaṇam api  RUnm 
yathā vā
na bhrūlatāṃ kuṭilaya kṣipa naiva hastaṃ
vaktraṃ ca kaṇṭakitagaṇḍam idaṃ na rundhi 
prīṇātu sundari tavādharabandhujīve
pītvā madhuni madhure madhusūdno'sau  RUnm 
atha bibbokaḥ
bibboko mānagarvābhyāṃ syād abhīṣṭe'py anādaraḥ  RUnm 
tatra garveṇa yathā
priyoktilakṣeṇa vipakṣasannidhau
svīkāritāṃ paśya śikhaṇḍamaulinā 
śyāmātivāmā hṛdayaṅgamām api
srajaṃ darāghrāya nirāsa helayā  RUnm 
yathā vā
sphuraty agre tiṣṭhan sakhi tava mukhaksiptanayanaḥ
pratīkṣāṃ kṛtvāyaṃ bhavadavasarasyāghadamanaḥ 
dṛśoccair gāmbhīryagrathitaguruhelāgahanayā
hasantīva kṣīve tvam iha vanamālāṃ racayasi  RUnm 
mānena yathā
hariṇā sakhi cāṭumaṇḍalīṃ
kriyamāṇām avamanya manyutaḥ 
na vṛthādya suśikṣitām api
svayam adhyāpaya gauri śārikām  RUnm 
atha lalitam
vinyāsabhaṅgiraṅgānāṃ bhrūvilāsamanoharāḥ 
sukumārā bhaved yatra lalitaṃ tadudīritam  RUnm 
yathā
subhrūbhaṅgam ananaṅgabāṇajananīr ālokayantī latāḥ
sollāsaṃ padapaṅkaje diśi diśi preṅkholayanty ujjvalā 
gandhākṛṣṭadhiyaḥ kareṇa mṛdunā vyādhunvatī ṣaṭpadān
rādhā nandati kuñjakandarataṭe vṛndāvanaśrīr iva  RUnm 
atha vikṛtam
hrīmānerṣyādibhir yatra nocyate svavivakṣitam 
vyajyate ceṣṭayaivedaṃ vikṛtaṃ tad vidur budhāḥ  RUnm 
tatra hriyā yathā
niśamayya mukunda manmukhā
dbhavadabhyarthitam atra sundarī 
na girābhinanda kintu sā
pulakenaiva kapolaśobhinā  RUnm 
yathā vā
na parapuruse dṛṣṭiksepo varākṣi tavocita
stvam asi kulajā sādhvī vaktraṃ prasīda vivartaya 
iti pathi mayā narmaṇy ukte harer navavīkṣaṇe
sadayam udayatkārpaṇyaṃ mām avaikṣata rādhikā  RUnm 
mānena yathā
mayāsaktavati prasādanavidhau vismṛtya candragrahaṃ
tadvijñaptisamutsukāpi vijahau maunaṃ na sā māninī 
kintu śyāmalaratnasampuṭadalenāvṛtya kiñcin mukhaṃ
satyā smārayati sma vismṛtam asau mām auparāgīṃ śriyam  RUnm 
īrsyayā yathā
vitara taskari me muralīṃ hṛtā
miti maduddharajalpavivṛttayā 
bhrūkuṭibhaṅguram arkasutātaṭe
sapadi rādhikayāham udīkṣitaḥ  RUnm 
alaṅkārā nigaditā viṃśatir gātracittajāḥ 
amī yathocitaṃ jñeyā mādhave'pi manīṣibhiḥ  RUnm 
kaiścid anye'py alaṅkārāḥ proktā nātra mayoditāḥ 
muner asammatatvena kintu dvitayam ucyate 
maugdhyaṃ ca cakitaṃ ceti kiñcin mādhuryapoṣaṇāt  RUnm 
tatra maugdhyam
jñātasyāpy ajñavat pṛcchā priyāgre maugdhyam īritam  RUnm 
yathā muktācarite
kās tā latāḥ kva vā santi kena vā kila ropitāḥ 
nātha matkaṅkaṇanyastaṃ yāsāṃ muktāphalaṃ phalam  RUnm 
cakitam
priyāgre cakitaṃ bhīter asthāne'pi bhayaṃ mahat  RUnm 
yathā
rakṣa rakṣa muhur eṣa bhīṣaṇo
dhāvati śravaṇacampakaṃ mama 
ity udīrya madhupād viśaṅkitā
sasvaje hariṇalocanā harim  RUnm 
ity alaṅkāravivṛtiḥ
atha udbhāsvarāḥ
udbhāsante svadhānīti proktā udbhāsvarā budhaiḥ  RUnm 
nīvyuttarīyadhammillasraṃsanaṃ gātramoṭanam 
jṛmbhā ghrāṇasya phullatvaṃ niśvāsādyāś ca te matāḥ  RUnm 
tatra nīvisraṃsanaṃ
yathā vidagdhamādhave
nairañjanyam upeyatuḥ parigalanmodāśruṇī locane
svedoddhūtavilepanaṃ kila kucadvandvaṃ jahau rāgitām 
yogautsukyam agād uraḥ sphurad iti prekṣyodayaṃ saṅgināṃ
rādhe nīvir iyaṃ tava ślathaguṇā śaṅke mumukṣāṃ dadhe  RUnm 
uttarīyasraṃsanaṃ yathā
tava hṛdi mama rāgāt ko'pi rāgo gariṣṭhaḥ
sphurati tad apasṛtya vyaktam etaṃ karomi 
iti khalu hṛdayāt te rādhike rodhakāri
cyutam iva purato me mañju māñjiṣṭhavāsaḥ  RUnm 
dhammillasraṃsanaṃ yathā
sphurati muradviṣi purato
durātmanām api vimuktide gauri 
nādbhutam idaṃ yadīyuḥ
saṃyaminas te kacā muktim  RUnm 
gātramoṭanaṃ yathā
vrajāṅgane vallavapuṅgavasya
puraḥ kuraṅgīnayanā salīlam 
apy aṅgabhaṅgaṃ kila kurvatīya
manaṅgabhaṅgaṃ tarasā vyatānīt  RUnm 
jṛmbhā yathā
puṣpair avetya viśikhair bhavatīm asādhyāṃ
sādhvīm adhītya madanaḥ kila jṛmbhaṇāstrām 
candrāvali prasabham eva vaśīcakāra
yad goṣṭhasīmani muhuḥ sakhi jṛmbhase'dya  RUnm 
ghrāṇaphullatvaṃ yathā
racitaśikharaśobhārambham ambhoruhākṣī
śvasitapavanadolāndolinā mauktikena 
puṭayugam atiphullaṃ bibhratī nāsikāyāṃ
mama manasi vilagnā darśanād eva rādhā  RUnm 
yadyapy ete viśeṣāḥ syur moṭṭāyitavilāsayoḥ 
śobhāviśeṣapoṣitvāt tathāpi pṛthag īritāḥ  RUnm 
atha vācikāḥ
ālāpaś ca vilāpaś ca saṃlāpaś ca pralāpakaḥ 
anulāpo'palāpaś ca sandeśaś cātideśakaḥ  RUnm 
apadeśopadeśau ca nirdeśo vyapadeśakaḥ 
kīrtitā vacanārambhā dvādaśāmī manīṣibhiḥ  RUnm 
tatra ālāpaḥ
cāṭupriyoktir ālāpaḥ  RUnm 
yathā śrīdaśame
kā stry aṅga te kalapadāyatamūrcchitena
sammohitā ryapadavīṃ na calet trilokyām 
trailokyasaubhagam idaṃ ca nirīkṣya rūpaṃ
yad godvijadrumamṛgān pulakāny abibhrat  RUnm 
yathā vā vidagdhamādhave 
kaṭhorā bhava mṛdvī vā prāṇās tvam asi rādhike 
asti nānyā cakorasya candralekhāṃ vinā gatiḥ  RUnm 
atha vilāpaḥ
vilāpo duḥkhajaṃ vacaḥ  RUnm 
yathā śrīdaśame 
paraṃ saukhyaṃ hi nairāśyaṃ svairiṇy apy āha piṅgalā 
taj jānatīnāṃ naḥ kṛṣṇe tathāpy āśā duratyayā  RUnm 
saṃlāpaḥ 
uktipratyuktimadvākyaṃ saṃlāpa iti kīrtyate  RUnm 
yathā padyāvalyāṃ 
uttiṣṭhārāt tarau me taruṇi mama taroḥ śaktir ārohaṇe kā
sākṣād ākhyāmi mugdhe taraṇim iha raver ākhyayā kā ratir me 
vārteyaṃ nauprasaṅge katham api bhavitā nāvayoḥ saṅgamārthā
vārtāpīti smitāsyaṃ jitagirim ajitaṃ rādhayārādhayāmi  RUnm 
pralāpaḥ 
vyarthālāpaḥ pralāpaḥ syāt  RUnm 
yathā
karoti nādaṃ muralī ralī ralī
vrajāṅganāhṛnmathanaṃ thanaṃ thanam 
tato vidūnā bhajate jate jate
hare bhavantaṃ lalitā litā litā  RUnm 
anulāpaḥ
anulāpo muhur vacaḥ  RUnm 
yathā
kṛṣṇaḥ kṛṣṇo nahi nahi tāpiñcho'yaṃ
veṇur veṇur nahi nahi bhṛṅgodghoṣaḥ 
guñjā guñjā nahi nahi bandhūkālī
netre netre nahi nahi padmadvandvam  RUnm 
apalāpaḥ 
apalāpas tu pūrvoktasyānyathā yojanaṃ bhavet  RUnm 
yathā
phullojjvalavanamālaṃ kāmayate kā na mādhavaṃ pramadā 
haraye spṛhayasi rādhe nahi nahi vairiṇi vasantāya  RUnm 
sandeśaḥ
sandeśas tu proṣitasya svavārtāpreṣaṇaṃ bhavet  RUnm 
yathā
vyāhara mathurānāthe mama sandeśaprahelikāṃ pāntha 
vikalā kṛtā kuhūbhir labhate candrāvalī kva layam  RUnm 
atideśaḥ
so'tideśas tad uktāni maduktānīti yad vacaḥ  RUnm 
yathā
vṛthā vṛthās tvaṃ vicikitsitāni
mā gokulādhīśvaranandanātra 
gāndharvikāyā giram antarasthāṃ
vīṇeva gītiṃ lalitā vyanakti  RUnm 
atha apadeśaḥ
anyārthakathanaṃ yat tu so'padeśa itīritaḥ  RUnm 
yathā
yat te vikṣatam ujjvalaṃ pṛthuphaladvandvaṃ navā dāḍimī
bhṛṅgeṇa vraṇitaṃ madhūni pibatā tāmraṃ ca puṣpadvayam 
ity ākarṇya sakhīgiraṃ gurujanāloke kila śyāmalā
cailena stanayor yugaṃ vyavadadhe dantacchadau pāṇinā  RUnm 
upadeśaḥ
yat tu śikṣārthavacanam upadeśaḥ sa ucyate  RUnm 
yathā chandomañjaryām
mugdhe yauvanalakṣmīr vidyudvibhramalolā
trailokyādbhutarūpo govindo'tidurāpaḥ 
tadvṛndāvanakuñje guñjadbhṛṅgasanāthe
śrīnāthena sametā svacchandaṃ kuru kelim  RUnm 
nirdeśaḥ
nirdeśas tu bhavet so'yam aham ity ādibhāṣaṇam  RUnm 
yathā
seyaṃ me bhaginī rādhā laliteyaṃ ca me sakhī 
viśākheyam ahaṃ kṛṣṇa tisraḥ puṣpārtham āgatāḥ  RUnm 
vyapadeśaḥ
vyājenātmābhilāṣoktir vyapadeśa itīryate  RUnm 
yathā
vilasannavakastavakā kāmyavane paśya mālatī milati 
katham iva cumbasi tumbīm athavā bhramaro'si kiṃ brūmaḥ  RUnm 
anubhāvā bhavanty ete rase sarvatra vācikāḥ 
mādhuryādhikyapoṣitvād ihaiva parikīrtitāḥ  RUnm 
iti śrīśrīujjvalanīlamaṇau anubhāvaprakaraṇam  
atha sāttvikaprakaraṇam
tatra stambhaḥ
sa harṣād
yathā dānakelikaumudyām 
abhyukṣya niṣkaṃ patayālunā muhuḥ
svedena niṣkampatayā vyavasthitā 
pañcālikā kuñcitalocanā kathaṃ
pañcālikādharmam avāpa rādhikā  RUnm 
bhayād yathā
ghanastanitacakreṇa cakiteyaṃ ghanastanī 
babhūva harim āliṅgya niścalāṅgī vrajāṅganā  RUnm 
 digdho'yam 
āścaryād yathā
tava madhurimasampadaṃ vilakṣa
trijagadalakṣyatulāṃ mukunda rādhā 
kalaya hṛdi balavaccamatkriyāsau
samajani nirnimiṣā ca niścalā ca  RUnm 
viṣādād yathā
vilambam ambhoruhalocanasya

atha svedaḥ

dravatāṃ svedabharacchalād bibharti  RUnm

mā bhūr viśākhe taralā vidūrataḥ
patis tavāsau niviḍā latākuṭi

atha romāñcaḥ 
sa āścaryād yathā

atha svarabhaṅgaḥ
sa viṣādād yathā śrīgītagovinde

rasajalanidhimagnā dhyānalagnā mṛgakṣī  RUnm

gurusambhramastimitakaṇṭhayā mayā
karasaṃjñayāpi bahudhāvabodhitā 
na punas tvam atra hariveṇuvādane
pulakān vilokitavatī latāsv api  RUnm 
amarṣād yathā
preyasyaḥ paramādbhutāḥ kati na me dīvyanti goṣṭhāntare
tāsāṃ nojjvalanarmabhaṅgibhir api prāpto'smi tuṣṭiṃ tathā 
dvitrair adya muhus taraṅgadadharagrastārdhavarṇair yathā
rādhāyāḥ sakhi roṣagadgadapadair ākṣepavāgbindubhiḥ  RUnm 
harṣād yathā śrīrukmiṇīsvayaṃvare
paśyema taṃ bhūya iti bruvāṇāṃ
sakhīṃ vacobhiḥ kila sā tatarja 
na prītikarṇejapatāṃ gatāni
vidāmbabhūva smaravaikṛtāni  RUnm 
bhīter yathā
prathamasaṅgamanarmaṇi sādhvasa
skhalitayāpi girā sakhi rādhikā 
navasudhāhradinīṃ madirekṣaṇā
śrutitaṭe mama kāñcid avīvahat  RUnm 
atha vepathuḥ
sa trāsena yathā
keśavo yuvativeśabhāg ayaṃ
bāliśaḥ kila patis tavāgrataḥ 
rādhike tad api mūrtir adya te
kiṃ pravātakadalītulāṃ dadhe  RUnm 
amarṣeṇa yathā
yadi kupitāsi na padme
kiṃ tunur utkampate prasabham 
vicalati kuto nivāte
dīpaśikhā nirbharasnigdhā  RUnm 
harṣeṇa yathā
vallavarājakumāre
milite purataḥ kim āttakampāsi 
tava peśalāsmi pārśve
laliteyaṃ pariharātaṅkam  RUnm 
atha vaivarṇyam
tadviṣādād yathā
madhurimabharair muktasyālaṃ kalaṅkitakuṅkumair
rdviradaradanaśreṇīm ābhāṃ cirāya vitanvataḥ 
vidhur api tulām āptas tasyā mukhasya bakīripo
vada param ataḥ sāraṅgyākṣyāḥ kim asti viḍambanam  RUnm 
roṣād yathā
vilasati kila vṛndāraṇyalīlāvihāre
kathaya katham akāṇḍe tāmravaktrāsi vṛttā 
prasaradudayarāgagrastapūrṇendubimbā
kim iva sakhi niśīthe śāradī jāyate dyauḥ  RUnm 
bhīter yathā
krīḍantyās taṭabhuvi mādhavena sārdhaṃ
tatrārāt patim avalokya viklavāyāḥ 
rādhāyās tanum anu kālimā tathāsīt
teneyaṃ kim api yathā na paryacāyi  RUnm 
atha aśru tatra harṣād
yathā śrīgītagovinde 
atikramyāpāṅgaṃ śravaṇapathaparyantagamana

idānīṃ rādhāyāḥ priyatamasamālokasamaye
papāta svedāmbuprasara iva harṣāśrunikaraḥ  RUnm 
phullagaṇḍaṃ saromāñcaṃ bāṣpam ānandajaṃ matam  RUnm 
roṣād yathā
prātar muradviṣam uraḥsphuradanyanārī
patrāṅkuraprakaralakṣmaṇam īkṣamāṇā

roṣāśrubindubharam indumukhī mumoca  RUnm 
yathā vā bilvamaṅgale
rādhe'parādhena vinaiva kasmād
asmāsu vācaḥ paruṣā ruṣā te 
aho kathaṃ te kucayoḥ prathante
hārānukārās taralāśrudhārāḥ  RUnm 
śiraḥkampi saniśvāsaṃ sphuradoṣṭhakapolakam

viṣādād yathā padyāvalyām 
malinaṃ nayanāñjanāmbubhir

karuṇāvaruṇālayo haris
tvayi bhūyaḥ karuṇāṃ vidhāsyati  RUnm 
atha pralayaḥ
sa sukhena yathā
jaṅghe sthāvaratāṃ gate parihṛtaspandā dvayī netrayoḥ
kaṇṭha kuṇṭhitaanisvano vighaṭitaśvāsā ca nāsāpuṭī 
rādhāyāḥ paramapramodasudhayā dhautaṃ puro mādhave
sākṣātkāram ite mano'pi munivan manye samādhiṃ dadhe  RUnm 
duḥkhena yathā lalitamādhave 
daṃśaḥ kaṃsanṛpasya vakṣasi ruṣā kṛṣṇorageṇārpyatāṃ
dūre goṣṭhataḍāgajīvanam ito yenāpajahre hariḥ 
hā dhik kaḥ śaraṇaṃ bhaven mṛdi luṭhadgātrīyam antaḥklamād
ābhīrīśapharītatiḥ śithilitaśvāsormir āmīlati  RUnm 
atha eṣu dhūmāyitāḥ
surāṅgane sakhi madhurāpur āṅgane
puraḥ purātanapuruṣasya vīkṣayā 
tavākṣiṇī jalakaṇasākṣiṇī kutaḥ
kathaṃ punaḥ pulaki ca gaṇḍamaṇḍalam  RUnm 
jvalitāḥ
sakhi stabdhībhāvaṃ bhajati nitarām uruyugalaṃ

prapannas te diṣṭyā nalinamukhi nīlo nidhir abhūt  RUnm

manye mādhavamādhurīśravaṇayor abhyāsam abhyāyayau  RUnm 
uddīptāḥ
snātā netrajanirjhareṇa dadhatī svedāmbumuktāvaliṃ

yathā
svedair darśiadurdinā vidadhatī bāṣpābubhir nistṛṣo

iti śrīśrīujjvalanīlamaṇau sāttvikaprakaraṇam  
atha vyabhicāriprakaraṇam
nirvedādyāstrayastriṃśadbhāvā ye parikīrtitāḥ

tatra nirvedaḥ
sa mahārtyā
yathā vidagdhamādhave

dharmaḥ so'pi mahān mayā na gaṇitaḥ sādhvībhir adhyāsito
dhig dhairyaṃ tadupekṣitāpi yad ahaṃ jīvāmi pāpīyasī  RUnm 
viprayogeṇa

atha viṣādaḥ 
sa iṣṭānavāptito

yair vā nipītam anuraktakaṭākṣamokṣam  RUnm 
prārabdhakāryāsiddher
yathā śrīgītagovinde

aparādhād yathā

atha dainyam 
tad duḥkhena

atha garvaḥ

yathā vā śrīdaśame

gaṇḍasthalaṃ śiśirahāsakaṭākṣamokṣaiḥ

parakrauryād
