mṛdvīm alabdhakusumāṃ nalinīṃ tvam enāṃ
mā kṛṣṇakuñjara kareṇa parispṛśādya  RUnm 
yathā vā śrīgītagovinde 
rāsollāsabhareṇa vibhramabhṛtām ābhīravāmabhruvām
abhyarṇaṃ parirabhya nirbharam uraḥ premāndhayā rādhayā 
sādhu tvadvadanaṃ sudhāmayam iti vyāhṛtya gītastuti
vyājād udbhaṭacumbitaḥ smṛtamanohāri hariḥ pātu vaḥ  RUnm 
dveṣeṇa yathā
yātu vakṣasi harer guṇasaṅga
projjhitā layam iyaṃ vanamālā 
yā kadāpy akhilasaukhyapadaṃ naḥ
kaṇṭham asya kuṭilā na jahāti  RUnm 
atha nidrā  sā klamena yathā
śvāsaspandanabandhurodaratalaṃ puṣpāvalīsrastara
nyañcanmauktikahārayaṣṭi kalayan nīvīṃ manāg ākulām 
klāntaḥ kelibharād urojakalasīm ābhīravāmabhruvaḥ
kalyāṇīm upadhāya sāndrapulakām adrau nidadrau hariḥ  RUnm 
yathā vā haṃsadūte 
alinde kālindīkamalasurabhau kuñjavasater
vasantīṃ vāsantī navaparimalodgāricikurām 
tvadutsaṅge nidrāsukhamukulitākṣīṃ punar imāṃ
kadāhaṃ seviṣye kiśalayakalāpavyajaninī  RUnm 
atha suptir yathā
puraḥ panthānaṃ me tyaja yad amunā yāmi yamunā
miti vyākṣāṇā cucukavicaratkaustubharuciḥ 
hareḥ savyaṃ rādhā bhujam upadadhaty ambujamukhī
darīkroḍe klāntā niviḍam iha nidrābharam agāt  RUnm 
yathā vā
ābhīrendrasutasya gaṇḍamukure svāpnībhir ullāsitaṃ
līlābhiḥ pulakaṃ vilokya cakitā niścinvatī jāgaram 
sā veṇor haraṇotsave dhṛtanavotkaṇṭhāpi talpāñcale
visrastaṃ karato'pi mādhyavasasau taṃ hartum eṇekṣaṇā  RUnm 
prabodhaḥ yathā
nidrāpramodaharam apy urukaṇṭhanādaṃ
kaṇṭhīravasya śitikaṇṭhapatatramauliḥ 
tuṣṭāva satvaravibuddhapariplavākṣa
rādhāpayodharagirindranipīḍitāṅgam  RUnm 
sakhyāṃ svasneho yathā
śailamūrdhni hariṇā viharantī
romakuḍmalakarmabitamūrtiḥ 
rādhikā salalitaṃ lalitāyāḥ
paśya mārṣṭi lulitālakam āsyam  RUnm 
atha utpattyādidaśācatuṣṭayam
tatra utpattir yathā
mṛdur iyam iti vādīr mā tvam asyā kuḍuṅge
śaśimukhi tava sakhyāḥ pauruṣaṃ dṛṣṭam asti 
iti bhavadupakaṇṭhe madgirā bhugnadṛṣṭeḥ
sthapuṭitavadanāyā rādhikāyāḥ smarāmi  RUnm 
atrāsūyotpattiḥ 
atha sandhiḥ 
tatra sarūpayor yathā
cirābhīṣṭe prekṣe danujadamane vidnati dṛśoḥ
padaṃ patyau cārdhasphuṭavacasi raktatviṣi ruṣā 
iyaṃ nispandāṅgī nimiṣakalanonmuktanayanā
babhūvāvaṣṭambhapratikṛtir ivābmhojavadanā  RUnm 
atreṣṭāniṣṭekṣaṇakṛtayor jāḍyayoḥ sandhiḥ 
atha bhinnayoḥ 
tatra ekahetujayor
yathā lalitamādhave 
śikharibharavitarkataḥ prataptaṃ
samaham aharniśam īkṣayā priyasya 
hṛdayam iha samastavallavīnāṃ
yugapad apūrvavidhaṃ dvidhā babhūva  RUnm 
atra viṣādaharṣayoḥ 
bhinnahetujayor yathā
sthavayati navarāgaṃ mādhave rādhikāyāṃ
giram atha lalitāyāḥ sāvahelāṃ pratītya 
calataracaraṇāgreṇālikhantī dharitrīṃ
vidhṛtavadanapadmā tatra siṣveda padmā  RUnm 
atra cintāmarṣayoḥ 
atha śāvalyam
yathā vidagdhamādhave 
dhanyās tā hariṇīdṛśaḥ sa ramate yābhir navīno yuvā
svairaṃ cāpalam ākalayya laltā māṃ hanta nindiṣyati 
govindaṃ parirabdhum induvadanaṃ hā cittam utkaṇṭhate
dhig vāmaṃ vidhim astu yena garalaṃ mānābhidhaṃ nirmame  RUnm 
atra cāpalaśaṅkautsukyāmarṣāṇāṃ śāvalyam 
atha śāntiḥ yathā
ālīyuktikuṭhārikāpaṭimābhir yo na prapede chidāṃ
dūtījalpitanirjhareṇa ca ciraṃ yaḥ kvāpi noccālitaḥ 
vaṃśnādamarullavena kamalācetas taṭīveṣṭano
mānākhyaḥ prabalonnatis tarur ayaṃ na kṣipram unmūlyate  RUnm 
atrerṣyākhyabhāvasya śāntiḥ 
iti śrīśrīujjvalanīlamaṇau
vyabhicāriprakaraṇam  
Many of the kārikās in this chapter are lifted pretty much wholesale from
Rasārṇavasudhākara I don't have the text with me
so I have not been able to give
the references
atha sthāyibhāvaprakaraṇam
sthāyibhāvo'tra śṛṅgāre kathyate madhurā ratiḥ  RUnm 
sā yathā govindavilāse
kālāhivaktravilasadrasanāgrajāgrad
gopīdṛgañcalacamatkṛtibiddhamarmā 
śarmādiśatv aruṇaghūrṇitalocanāntaḥ
sañcāracūrṇitasatīhṛdayo mukundaḥ  RUnm 
yathā vā dānakelikaumudyām 
govardhanagirim upetya kaṭākṣabāṇān
karṇasphuranmaṇizilopari saṅkṣuvānā 
kā bhrūdhanurdhuvanasūcitaluñcaneyaṃ
vyagrīkaroty ahaha mām api sambhrameṇa  RUnm 
abhiyogād viṣayataḥ sambandhād abhimānataḥ 
sā tadīyaviśeṣebhya upamātaḥ svabhāvataḥ 
ratir āvirbhaved eṣām uttamatvaṃ yathottaram  RUnm 
tatra abhiyogaḥ
abhiyogo bhaved bhāvavyaktiḥ svena pareṇa ca  RUnm 
tatra svenābhiyogād yathā
madadharaviluṭhadvilocanāntaṃ
mṛdulalatānavapallavaṃ daśantam 
sakhi harim avalokya bhānujāyā
staṭavipine sphuṭadantarāsmi jātā  RUnm 
yathā vā
kuvalayavipināny asau sṛjantī
diśi diśi locanacāpalāc calākṣī 
harati taraṇijātaṭe puraḥ kā
subala balān mama cittacañcarīkam  RUnm 
pareṇābhiyogād yathā
tvadīyam āpīya gatāvalambā
saṃvādamādhvīkam atīva sādhvī 
āghūrṇamānā vrajarājasūno
nīvīṃ skhalantīṃ na vidāñcakāra  RUnm 
atha viṣayāḥ
śabdasparśādayaḥ pañca viṣayāḥ kila viśrutāḥ  RUnm 
tatra śabdād
yathā vidagdhamādhave 
nādaḥ kadambaviṭapāntarato visarpan
ko nāma karṇapadavīm aviśan na jāne 
hā hā kulīnagṛhiṇīgaṇagarhaṇīyāṃ
yenādya kām api daśāṃ sakhi lambhitāsi  RUnm 
yathā vā tatraiva 
ekasya śrutam eva lumpati matiṃ kṛṣṇeti nāmākṣaraṃ
sāndronmādaparamparām apanayaty anyasya vaṃśīkalaḥ 
eṣa snigdhaghanadyutir manasi me lagnā sakṛdvīkṣaṇāt
kaṣṭaṃ dhik puruṣatraye ratir abhūn manye mṛtiḥ śreyasī  RUnm 
sparśād yathā
vrajaṃ muṣṭigrāhye tamasi nigiraty aṅgam iha me
sakhi sparśaṃ daivād yadavadhi paraṃ kasyacid agāt 
gṛhītā jāgaryā tadavadhi sadaivāṅgajagaṇaiḥ
saśaṅkair yā paśya kṣaṇam api na sādyānpy uparatā  RUnm 
rūpād yathā haṃsadūte 
kṛtākṛṣṭikrīḍaṃ kim api tava rūpaṃ mama sakhī
sakṛd dṛṣṭvā dūrād ahitahitabodhojjhitamatiḥ 
hatā seyaṃ premānalam anu viśantī sarabhasaṃ
pataṅgīvātmānaṃ murahara muhur dāhitavatī  RUnm 
rasād yathā
pulakayati yad aṅgaṃ sevate gātrabhaṅgaṃ
vahati hṛdi taraṅgaṃ sadya evādya mugdhā 
tad aghadamanavaktrodgīrṇatāmbūlam alpaṃ
sphuṭam aviditam āsye nyastam asyās tvayāli  RUnm 
gandhād yathā
vibhrājante kva sakhi sukhinaḥ śākhino mohanās te
yeṣāṃ puṣpair iyam anupamā vaijayantī kṛtāsti 
paśyākṛṣṭabhramarapaṭalā yātayāmāpi kāmaṃ
yā bhūyobhir mama parimalaiḥ stambhayaty adya cetaḥ  RUnm 
lokottarapadārthānāṃ prabhāvaḥ ko'py anargalaḥ 
ratiṃ tadviṣayaṃ cāsau bhāsayet tūrṇam ekadā  RUnm 
atha sambandhaḥ
sambandhaḥ kularūpādisāmagrīgauravaṃ bhavet  RUnm 
tato yathā
vīryaṃ kandukitādirrūpam akhilakṣmāmaṇḍalīmaṇḍanaṃ
janmābhīrapurandarasya bhavane pāreparārdhaṃ guṇāḥ 
līlā kvāpi jagaccamatkṛtikarīty etasya lokottarā
vṛttir veṇudharasya durmukhi dhṛtiṃ kasyāḥ kṣaṇaṃ rakṣati  RUnm 
atha abhimānaḥ
santu ramyāṇi bhūrīṇi prārthyaṃ syād idam eva me 
iti yo nirṇayo dhīrair abhimānaḥ sa ucyate  RUnm 
tato yathā
sphurantu bahavaḥ kṣitau madhurimormidhaureyakā
vidagdhamaṇayo guṇāvalipatiṃvarābhir vṛtāḥ 
na yasya śikhicandraṃ śirasi naiva veṇur mukhe
na dhātuvacanā tanau sakhi tṛṇāya manye na tam  RUnm 
atha tadīyaviśeṣāḥ
tadīyānāṃ viśeṣāḥ syuḥ padagoṣṭhapriyādayaḥ  RUnm 
tatra padāni
padāny atra padāṅkāḥ syuḥ  RUnm 
tato yathā
sphurati sakhi rathāṅgāmbhojadambholibhājāṃ
taṭabhuvi viśadeyaṃ kasya paṅktiḥ padānām 
hṛdayam aghṛṇaghūrṇāghrātam udghāṭayantī
mama tanulatikāyāṃ kuḍmalaṃ yā tanoti  RUnm 
atha goṣṭham
goṣṭhaṃ vṛndāvanāśritam  RUnm 
tato yathā
madayati hṛdayaṃ sakhi vrajo'yaṃ
madhurimabhiḥ kvacid apy adṛṣṭapūrvaiḥ 
iha viharati ko'pi nāgarendara
stribhuvanamaṇḍalamūrtir ity avehi  RUnm 
atha priyajanaḥ
prauḍhabhāvānubiddho yas tasya priyajano'tra saḥ  RUnm 
tato yathā
gurubhir niṣiddhā tām ahaṃ yāvad akṣṇoḥ
padam anayamanantaśreyasāṃ sadma rādhām 
tṛṣitam iva mano me prekṣate tanvi tāvad
diśi diśi viharantīṃ śyāmalāṃ śālabhañjīm  RUnm 
atha upamā
yathā kathañcid apy asya sādṛśyam upamoditā  RUnm 
tato yathā
navāmbudharamādhurī sphurati mūrtir urvītale
kṛśodari dṛśor iyāt pathi kim īdṛśo vā yuvā 
puraḥ sumukhi gopateḥ sadai sanniviṣṭasya me
pitur vitanute naṭo yam anukṛtya nṛtyakramam  RUnm 
yathā vā
sphuraty eṣa preyān iva navaghanas tasya subhage
śikhaṇḍīnāṃ śreṇīṃ tulayati surendrāyudham idam 
asau vāso lakṣmīr iva viharate vidyud iti sā
niśamyodasrākṣī tvayi nihitabuddhir nivasati  RUnm 
atha svabhāvaḥ
bhair hetvanapekṣī tu svabhāvo'rthaḥ prakīrtitaḥ 
nisargaś ca svarūpaṃ cety eṣo'pi bhavati dvidhā  RUnm 
atra nisargaḥ
nisargaḥ sudṛḍhābhyāsajanyaḥ saṃskara ucyate 
tadudbhodhasya hetuḥ syād guṇarūpaśrutir manāk  RUnm 
tato yathā
sa tarjatu batāgrajaṃ tyajatu māṃ suhṛnmaṇḍalaḥ
pitā kila vilajjatāṃ ghanadṛgambur ambāstu me 
manaḥ sakhi samīhate śrutaguṇaśriyaṃ sarvathā
tam eva yadupuṅgavaṃ na tu kadāpi caidyaṃ nṛpam  RUnm 
yathā vā
asundaraḥ sundaraśekharo vā
guṇair vihīno guṇināṃ varo vā 
dveṣī mayi syāt karuṇāmbudhir vā
śyāmaḥ sa evādya gatir mamāyam  RUnm 
atha svarūpam
ajanyas tu svataḥsiddhaḥ svarūpaṃ bhāva iṣyate 
etat tu kṛṣṇalalanobhayaniṣṭhatayā tridhā  RUnm 
atha kṛṣṇaniṣṭham
kṛṣṇaniṣṭhaṃ svarūpaṃ syād adaityaiḥ sugamaṃ janaiḥ  RUnm 
tato yathā
iyaṃ vyaktir gopī na bhavati puraḥ kintu kutukī
harir nārīveśo yad akhilasurastrīr dhuvati naḥ 
jagannetraśreṇītimiraharaṇāyāmbaramaṇiṃ
vinā kasyānyasya priyasakhi bhaved aupayikatā  RUnm 
atha lalanāniṣṭham
svarūpaṃ lalanāniṣṭhaṃ svayam udbuddhatāṃ vrajet 
adṛṣṭe'py aśrute'py uccaiḥ kṛṣṇe kuryād drutaṃ ratim  RUnm 
tato yathā
jihīte yaḥ kakṣāṃ kvacid alam adṛṣṭāśrutacara
trilokyām astīti kṣaṇam api na sambhāvanamayīm 
ghanaśyāmaṃ pītāmbaram ahaha saṅkalpayad amuṃ
janaṃ kañcid goṣṭhe sakhi mama vṛthā dīryati manaḥ  RUnm 
atha ubhayaniṣṭham
tat syād ubhayaniṣṭhaṃ yat svarūpaṃ kṛṣṇasubhruvoḥ  RUnm 
tato yathā lalitamādhave 
sahacari harir eṣa brahmaveśaṃ prapannaḥ
kim ayam itarathā me vidravaty antarātmā 
śaśadharamaṇivedī svedadhārāṃ prasūte
na kila kumudabandhoḥ kaumudīm antareṇa  RUnm 
proktā atrābhiyogādyā vilāsādhikyahetave 
ratiḥ svabhāvajaiva syāt prāyo gokulasubhruvām  RUnm 
sādhāraṇī nigaditā samañjasāsau samarthā ca 
kubjādiṣu mahiṣīṣu ca gokuladevīṣṇḍ ca kramataḥ  RUnm 
maṇivaccintāmaṇivatkaustubhamaṇivat tridhābhimatā 
nātisulabheyam abhitaḥ sudurlabhā syād ananyalabhyā ca  RUnm 
tatra sādhāraṇī
nātisāndrā hareḥ prāyaḥ sākṣād darśanasambhavā 
sambhogecchānidāneyaṃ ratiḥ sādhāraṇī matā  RUnm 
yathā śrīdaśame 
sahoṣyatām iha preṣṭha dināni katicin mayā 
ramasva notsahe tyaktuṃ saṅgaṃ te'mburuhekṣaṇa  RUnm 
asāndratvād rater asyāḥ sambhogecchā vibhidyate 
etasyā hrāsato hrāsas taddhetutvād rater api  RUnm 
atha samañjasā
patnībhāvābhimānātmā guṇādiśravaṇādijā 
kvacid bheditasambhogatṛṣṇā sāndrā samañjasā  RUnm 
yathā tatraiva 
kā tvā mukunda mahatī kulaśīlarūpa
vidyāvayodraviṇadhāmabhir ātmatulyam 
dhīrā patiṃ kulavatī na vṛṇīta kanyā
kāle nṛsiṃha naralokamano'bhirāmam  RUnm 
samañjasātaḥ sambhogaspṛhāyā bhinnatā yadā 
tadā tadutthitair bhāvair vaśyatā duṣkarā hariḥ  RUnm 
tathā hi tatraiva 
smāyāvalokalavadarśitabhāvahāri
bhrūmaṇḍalaprahitasauratamantraśauṇḍaiḥ 
patnyas tu ṣoḍaśasahasram anaṅgabāṇair
yasyendriyaṃ vimathituṃ karaṇair na śekuḥ  RUnm 
atha samarthā
kaṃcid viśeṣam āyantyā sambhogecchā yayābhitaḥ 
ratyā tādātmyam āpannā sā samartheti bhaṇyate  RUnm 
svasvarūpāt tadīyād vā jātā yatkiṃcidanvayāt 
samarthā sarvavismārigandhā sāndratamā matā  RUnm 
prekṣyāśeṣe jagati madhurāṃ svāṃ vadhūṃ śaṅkayā te
tasyāḥ pārśve gurubhir abhitas tvatprasaṅgo nyavāri 
śrutvā dūre tad api bhavataḥ sā tulākoṭinādaṃ
hā kṛṣṇety aśrutacaram api vyāharanty unmadāsīt  RUnm 
sarvādbhutavilāsormicamatkārakaraśriyaḥ 
sambhogecchāviśeṣo'syā rater jātu na bhidyate 
ity asyāṃ kṛṣṇasaukhyārtham eva kevalam udyamaḥ  RUnm 
pūrvasyāṃ svasukhāyāpi kadācit tatra sambhavet  RUnm 
iyam eva ratiḥ prauḍhā mahābhāvadaśāṃ vrajet 
yā mṛgyā syād vimuktānāṃ bhaktānāṃ ca varīyasām  RUnm 
yathā śrīdaśame 
etāḥ paraṃ tanubhṛto bhuvi gopavadhvo
govinda eva nikhilātmani rūḍhabhāvāḥ 
vāñchanti yad bhavabhiyo munayo vayaṃ ca
kiṃ brahmajanmabhir anantakathārasasya  RUnm 
syād dṛḍheyaṃ ratiḥ premā prodyan snehaḥ kramād ayam 
syān mānaḥ praṇayo rāgo'nurāgo bhāva ity api  RUnm 
bījam ikṣuḥ sa ca rasaḥ sa guḍaḥ khaṇḍa eva saḥ 
sa śarkarā sitā sā ca sā yathā syāt sitopalā  RUnm 
ataḥ premavilāsāḥ syur bhāvāḥ snehādayas tu ṣaṭ 
prāyo vyavahiryante'mī premaśabdena sūribhiḥ  RUnm 
yasyā yādṛśajātīyaḥ kṛṣṇe premābhyudañcati 
tasyāṃ tādṛśajātīyaḥ sa kṛṣṇasyāpy udīyate  RUnm 
tatra premā
sarvathā dhvaṃsarahitaṃ saty api dhvaṃsakāraṇe 
yadbhāvabandhanaṃ yūnoḥ sa premā parikīrtitaḥ  RUnm 
yathā
śape tubhyaṃ dharmasthitimanyusarantyā sakhi mayā
viśuddhām ugrābhir muhur api nirasto bhaṇitibhiḥ 
sa mugdhe śyāmātmā tyajati na hi me vartma bata māṃ
jagārāpadghorā viracayatu śāstiṃ gṛhapatiḥ  RUnm 
yathā vā
rādhāyāḥ sakhi sadguṇair anudinaṃ rūpānurāgādibhiḥ
sāndrāṃ labdhavator api vyasanitāṃ vyākṣiptakāntāntaraiḥ 
prāpa kvāpi parasparopari yayor na mlānatāṃ yas tayo
staṃ candrāvalicandrakābharaṇayoḥ ko vetti bhāvakramam  RUnm 
sa tridhā kathyate prauḍhamadhyamandaprabhedataḥ  RUnm 
tatra prauḍhaḥ
vilambādibhir ajñātacittavṛttau priye jane 
itarakleśakārī yaḥ sa premā prauḍha ucyate  RUnm 
yathā
gatvā brūhi nikuñjasadmani sakhe khinnāṃ mama preyasīṃ
mā kālātyayam ākalayya kamale mayy apratītiṃ kṛthāḥ 
duṣṭaṃ dānavam atra gokulaśiraḥśūlaṃ cikitsann ahaṃ
drāg eṣa praṇayena pallavamayīṃ labdho'smi śayyāṃ tava  RUnm 
atha madhyaḥ
itarānubhavāpekṣāṃ sahate yaḥ sa madhyamaḥ  RUnm 
yathā
sarvārambhamanoharāṃ sapadi me candrāvalīṃ vindato
raṅgaḥ śāradaśarvarīsamucitaḥ paryāptim evāyayau 
tāṃ kandarpacamūcamatkṛtikarakrīḍormikirmīritāṃ
rādhāṃ hanta tathāpi cittam adhunā sākṣān mamāpekṣate  RUnm 
atha mandaḥ
sadā paricitatvādeḥ karoty atyantikāt tu yaḥ 
naivopekṣāṃ na cāpekṣāṃ sa premā manda ucyate  RUnm 
yathā
anumīya rūḍhamānām ānaya bhāmāṃ sakhīm aśokalatām 
bhavati premavatīnāṃ manāg upekṣāpi doṣāya  RUnm 
athavā
prauḍhaḥ premā sa yatra syād viśleṣasyāsahiṣṇutā  RUnm 
yathā uddhavasandeśe 
nirmāya tvaṃ vitara phalakam hāri kaṃsārimūrtyā
vāraṃ vāraṃ diśasi yadi māṃ mānanirvāhanāya 
yat paśyantī bhavanakuhare ruddhakarṇāntarāhaṃ
sāhaṃkārā priyasakhi sukham yāpayiṣyāmi yāmam  RUnm 
kṛcchrāt sahiṣṇutā yatra sa tu madhyama ucyate  RUnm 
yathā
avitatham asau kiṃ drāghīyān gamiṣyati vāsaraḥ
sumukhi sa niśārambhaḥ kiṃvā sameṣyati maṅgalaḥ 
smitamukhaśaśī godhūlibhiḥ karambitakuntalaḥ
kṣapayati dṛśām ārtiṃ yatra vrajeśvaranandanaḥ  RUnm 
sa mandaḥ kathito yatra bhavet kutrāpi vismṛtiḥ  RUnm 
yathā
pratipakṣajanerṣyayā na me
smṛtir āsīd vanamālyagumphane 
sakhi kiṃ karavai gavāṃ puro
ghanahambādhvanir eṣa jṛmbhate  RUnm 
atha snehaḥ
āruhya paramāṃ kāṣṭhāṃ premā ciddīpadīpanaḥ 
hṛdayaṃ drāvayann eṣa sneha ity abhidhīyate 
atrodite bhavej jātu na tṛptir darśanādiṣu  RUnm 
yathā kramadīpikāyām 
tad atimadhurarūpakamraśobhā
mṛtarasapānavidhānalālasābhyām 
praṇayasalilapūravāhinīnām
alasavilolavilocanāmbujābhyām  RUnm 
yathā vā
jyotsnaśīdhuṃ harimukhavidhor apy analpaṃ pibantau
nāntas tṛptiṃ tava katham api prāpnuto dṛkcakorau 
āghūrṇantau madakalatayā suṣṭhu mugdhau yad etau
bhūyo bhūyas tam iha vamato bāṣpapūracchalena  RUnm 
aṅgasaṅge viloke ca śravaṇādau ca sa kramāt 
kaniṣṭho madhyamaḥ śreṣṭhas trividho'yaṃ manodravaḥ  RUnm 
tatra aṅgasaṅge yathā
asi ghanarasarūpas tvaṃ pālī lāvaṇyasāramayamūrtiḥ 
mādhava bhavadāśleṣe bhavitā nāsyāḥ kathaṃ dravatā  RUnm 
viloke yathā
asyās tvadvadane sarojasuhṛdi vyaktiṃ purastād gate
nāścaryaṃ dravatām avindata manohaiyaṅgavīnaṃ yadi 
kintv āścaryam idaṃ mukunda milite śyāmāmukhendau bhava
ccetaś candramaṇir dravan jalatayā bhūyo babhūvācalaḥ  RUnm 
śravaṇe yathā
śrutiparisarakakṣāṃ yāti nāmnas tavārdhe
muradamana dṛgambhodārayā dhautagātrī 
madanamadamadhūlīmugdhamedhāsamṛddhiḥ
skhalati kuvalayākṣī jṛmbhate stambhate ca  RUnm 
ādiśabdena smaraṇe yathā
kṛṣṇavartmani kṛtābhiniveśo
sāmprataḥ tvam asi kampitagātrī 
snehapūraparipākamayaṃ te
kiṃ bhaviṣyati mano na vilīnam  RUnm 
sa ghṛtaṃ madhu cetyuktaṃ sneho dvedhā svarūpataḥ  RUnm 
tatra ghṛtasnehaḥ
ātyantikādaramayaḥ sneho ghṛtam itīryate  RUnm 
bhāvāntarānvitao gacchan svādodrekaṃ na tu svayam 
ghanībhaven nisargātiśītalān mitha ādarāt 
gāḍhādaramayas tena snehaḥ syād ghṛtavad ghṛtam  RUnm 
yathā
abhutthāya vidūrato madhubhñdā yāśliṣyate sādaraṃ
yā snehena vaśīkaroti guruṇā pāvitryapūrṇena tam 
kṣipraṃ yāti sitopaleva vilayaṃ tatkelivṛṣṭyā ca yā
yuktā hanta kayopamātum api sā candrāvalī me sakhī  RUnm 
yathā vā
nijam agharipuṇāṃse nyastam ākṛṣya savyaṃ
bhujam iha nidadhānā dakṣam asrokṣitākṣī 
padayugam api baṅkaṃ śaṅkayā vikṣipantī
pratiyuvativayasyāṃ smerayāmāsa gaurī  RUnm 
ādaro gauravotthaḥ syād ity anyonyāśritadvayam 
ratyādau sad api snehe suvyaktatvād ihocyate  RUnm 
madīyatātiśayabhāk priye sneho bhaven madhu 
svayaṃ prakaṭamādhuryo nānārasasamāhṛtiḥ  RUnm 
mattatoṣmadharaḥ sneho madhusāmyān madhūcyate  RUnm 
yathā
rādhā snehamayena hanta racitā mādhuryasāreṇa sā
saudhīva pratimā ghanāpy uruguṇair bhāvoṣmaṇā vidrutā 
yannāmany api dhāmani śravaṇayor yāti prasaṅgena me
sāndrānandamayī bhavaty anupamā sadyo jagadvismṛti  RUnm 
atha mānaḥ
snehas tūtkṛṣṭatāvāptyā mādhuryaṃ mānayan navam 
yo dhārayaty adākṣiṇyaṃ sa māna iti kīrtyate  RUnm 
yathā
sravadasrabhare kṛte dṛśau me
tava godhūlibhir eva gopavīra 
adhunā vadanānilaiḥ kim ebhi
rvirameti bhrūkuṭiṃ babhāra subhrūḥ  RUnm 
udātto lalitaś ceti māno'yaṃ dvividho mataḥ  RUnm 
tatra udāttaḥ
udāttaḥ syād ghṛtasneho dhārayan gahanakramam 
dākṣiṇyabhāgadākṣiṇyaṃ vāmyagandhaṃ ca kutracit  RUnm 
tatra dākṣiṇyodātto yathā
rādheti skhilābhidhe mayi haṭhād biddhāntarāpy ārtibhir
madvailakṣyaśamāya sā dviguṇayanty āsyāravinde smitam 
jalpe ca mradimānubiddham adhikaṃ mādhuryam ātanvatī
citrāṇīva cakāra matpriyasuhṛdvṛnāni candrāvalī  RUnm 
atha vāmyagandhodātto
yathā śrīviṣṇupurāṇe 
kācid bhrūbhaṅguraṃ kṛtvā lalāṭaphalakaṃ harim 
vilokya netrabhṛṅgābhyāṃ papau tanmukhapaṅkajam  RUnm 
yathā vā
akṣasaṃsadi jitāpi mṛgākṣī
mādhavena parirambhapaṇena 
bhugnadṛṣṭir iha vipratipannāṃ
taṃ karaṇe rurudhe pariripsum  RUnm 
atha lalitaḥ
madhusnehas tu kauṭilyaṃ svātantryahṛdayaṅgamam 
bibhrannarmaviśeṣaṃ ca lalito'yam udīryate  RUnm 
tatra kauṭilyalalito
yathā śrīdaśame 
ekā bhrūkuṭim ābaddhya premasaṃrambhavihvalā 
ghnatīvaikṣat sandaṣṭadaśanacchadā  RUnm 
yathā vā
adatta me vartmani manmathonmadā
svayaṃgrahāśleṣam asau sakhī tava 
ity uktavantaṃ kuṭilībhavan mukhī
kṛṣṇaṃ vataṃsena jaghāna maṅgalā  RUnm 
yathā vā
citraṃ cirasparśasukhāya cucuke
kurvantam akṣipram iyaṃ calekṣaṇā 
svinnāṅgulīkaṃ pulakāñcitaśriyā
savyena cikṣepa kucena keśavam  RUnm 
atha narmalalito
yathā dānakelikaumudyām 
mithyā jalpatu te kathaṃ nu rasanā sādhvīsahasrasya yā
bimboṣṭhāmṛtasevanād agharipo puṇyā prayatnād abhūt 
kasmād eva balṃtkarotu ca karaḥ soḍhuṃ kṣamaḥ subhruvāṃ
raktaḥ suṣṭhu na nIvibandham api yaḥ kā vānyabandhe kathā  RUnm 
atha praṇayaḥ
māno dadhāno viśrambhaṃ praṇayaḥ procyate budhaiḥ  RUnm 
yathā
kucopānte spṛṣṭā muravijayinā tadbhujaśira
stironyastagrīvā bhruvam anṛjudṛṣṭir vibhujatī 
paṭenāsya mlānīkṛtapuraṭabhāsā pulakinī
pramodāsrair dhautaṃ nijamukham iyaṃ mārṣṭi sumukhī  RUnm 
svarūpaṃ praṇayasyāsya viśrambhaḥ kathito budhaiḥ 
viśrambho'pi dvidhā maitraṃ sakhyaṃ ceti nigadyate  RUnm 
tatra maitraṃ
bhāvajñaiḥ procyate maitraṃ viśrambho vinayānvitaḥ  RUnm 
yathā śrīdaśame 
kācit karāmbujaṃ śaurer jagṛhe'ñjalināṃ mudā 
kācid dadhāra tadbāhum aṃse candanarūṣitam  RUnm 
yathā vā
na hi saṅkuca paṅkajekṣaṇaḥ
pādayos te nidadhātu nūpurau 
anayor dhvanibhir vilajjatāṃ
kalahaṃsīva vipakṣakāminī  RUnm 
atha sakhyam
visrambhaṃ sādhvasonmuktaḥ sakhyaṃ svavaśatāmayaḥ  RUnm 
yathā
sarabhasam adhikaṇṭham arpitābhyāṃ
danujaripor nijabāhuvallarībhyām 
niṭilam avanamayya tasya karṇe
sakhi kathitaṃ kim iva tvayā rahasyam  RUnm 
yathā vā śrīviṣṇupurāṇe 
yadi te tadvacaḥ satyaṃ satyātyarthaṃ priyeti me 
madgehaniṣkuṭārthāya tadāyaṃ nīyatāṃ taruḥ  RUnm 
yathā vā
vinyasya vakṣoruhakorakadvayīṃ
vakṣaḥsthale kaṃsaharasya hāriṇīm 
patrāṅkuraṃ kuṅkumabindunālike
likhaty asau candramukhī sakhī mama  RUnm 
yathā vā śrīdaśame 
tato gatvā vanoddeśe dṛptā keśavam abravīt 
na pāraye'haṃ calituṃ naya māṃ yatra te manaḥ  RUnm 
janitvā praṇayaḥ snehāt kutracin mānatāṃ vrajet 
snehān mānaḥ kvacid bhūtvā praṇayatvam athāśnute  RUnm 
kāryakāraṇatānyon'nyam ataḥ praṇayamānayoḥ 
ity atra pṛthag evāsau viśrambhodāhṛtiḥ kṛtā  RUnm 
udāttalalitābhyāṃ tu maitryasakhye susaṅgate 
dve sumaitryasusakhyākhye yathāsaṅkhyam udīrite  RUnm 
tatra sumaitryam
ālīpuraḥ kathayituṃ rajanīrahasyaṃ
tatrodyate madhuripau mṛdulā bhramadbhrūḥ 
utkṣipya tan mukhapuṭāvaraṇāya hastaṃ
nyañcanmukhī samavariṣṭa punar varākṣī  RUnm 
yathā vā
kṣipte varṇakabhājane taraṇijāpure parīhāsataḥ
kṛṣṇena bhruvam āracayya kuṭilām ālokayantī tiraḥ 
tārā vakṣasi citram ardhalikhitaṃ śrīvatsavibhrājite
kāśmīreṇa ghanaśriyā nijakucākṛṣṭena pūrṇaṃ vyadhāt  RUnm 
atha susakhyam
dyūte sakṛt pānavidhau paṇīkṛte
jitvā dviroṣṭhaṃ pibati svam acyute 
babandha kaṇṭhe kuṭilīkṛtekṣaṇā
taṃ vāmayā dorlatayāsya vallavī  RUnm 
yathā vā
āviṣkurvati visphuran navanakhollekhaṃ svavakṣastaṭaṃ
kṛṣṇe pītadukūlasaṅkalanayā smitvā sakhīnāṃ puraḥ 
abhraśyāmam uro rurodha valitabhrūr ānanaṃ dhunvatī
romāñcodgamakañcukena kucayor dvandvena gāndharvikā  RUnm 
atha rāgaḥ
duḥkham apy adhikaṃ citte sukhatvenaiva rajyate 
yatas tu praṇayotkarṣāt sa rāga iti kīrtyate  RUnm 
yathā
tīvrārkadyutidīpitair asilatādhārākarālāsribhi
rmārtaṇḍopalamaṇḍalaiḥ sthapuṭite'py adres taṭe tasthuṣī 
paśyanti paśupendranandanam asāv indīvarair āstṛte
talpe nyastapadāmbujeva muditā na spandate rādhikā  RUnm 
yathā vā padyāvalyāṃ 
tārābhisāraka caturthaniśāśaśāṅka
kāmāmburāśiparivardhana deva tubhyam 
argho namo bhavatu me saha tena yūnā
mithyāpavādavacasāpy abhimānasiddhiḥ  RUnm 
nīlimā raktimā ceti rāgo'yaṃ dvividho mataḥ  RUnm 
tatra nīlimā
nīlīśyāmābhavo rāgo nīlimā kathyate budhaiḥ  RUnm 
tatra nīlīrāgaḥ
vyayasambhāvanāhīno bahir nātiprakāśavān 
svalagnabhāvāvaraṇo nīlīrāgaḥ satāṃ mataḥ 
yathāvalokyate caiṣa candrāvalimukundayoḥ  RUnm 
yathā
prasannaviśadāśayā vividhamudrayā nirmitaṃ
pratāraṇam api tvayā guṇatayā sadā gṛhṇatī 
tathā vyavajahāra sā vrajakulendra candrāvalī
sakhībhir api tarkitā tvayi yathā taṭasthety asau  RUnm 
atha śyāmārāgaḥ
bhīrutauṣadhisekādir ādyāt kiñcit prakāśabhāk 
yaś cireṇaiva sādhyaḥ syāt sa śyāmārāga ucyate  RUnm 
yathā
purā kuñje mañjuny avatamasayukte'pi cakitā
murārer yā pārśve na taruṇi divāpy antaram agāt 
tamālaiḥ saivādya dviguṇitatamisre'pi muditā
tamisrārdhe māniny ahaha bhavatī taṃ mṛgayate  RUnm 
atha raktimā
rāgaḥ kusumbhamañjiṣṭhāsambhavo raktimā mataḥ  RUnm 
tatra kusumbharāgaḥ
kusumbharāgaḥ sa jñeyo yaś citte sajjati drutam 
anyarāgacchavivyañjī śobhate ca yathocitam  RUnm 
yathā
tvayy eva śravaṇāvadhi priyasakhī yā kṛṣṇabaddhāntarā
yā dṛṣṭe bhujage'pi tāvakabhujāsāmyāt pramodonmadā 
prekṣya tvāṃ purato'dya kām api daśāṃ prātāsti seyaṃ tathā
na jñāyeta yathā kim eṣa balavān rāgo virāgo'thavā  RUnm 
sadādhāraviśeṣeṣu kausumbho'pi sthiro bhavet 
iti kṛṣṇapraṇayiṣu mlānir asya na yujyate  RUnm 
atha mañjiṣṭharāgaḥ
ahāryo'nanyasāpekṣo yaḥ kāntyā varddhate sadā 
bhaven māñjiṣṭharāgo'sau rādhāmādhavayor yathā  RUnm 
yathā
dhatte drāg anupādhi janma vidhinā kenāpi nākampate
sūte'ty āhitasañcayair api rasaṃ te cen mitho vartmane 
ṛddhiṃ sañcinute camatkṛtikaroddāmapramodottarāṃ
rādhāmādhavayor ayaṃ nirupamaḥ premānubandhotsavaḥ  RUnm 
yathā vā vidagdhamādhave 
mayā te nirbandhān murajayini rāgaḥ parihṛtya
mayi snigdhe kintu prathaya paramāśīs tatim imām 
mukhāmododgāragrahilamatir adyaiva hi yataḥ
pradoṣārambhe syāṃ vimalavanamālāmadhukarī  RUnm 
pūrvapūrvas tu yo bhāvaḥ somābhādau sa rājate 
tathā bhīṣmasutādau ca śrīharer mahiṣīgaṇe  RUnm 
ya uttarottaro dviyo rādhikādau sa dīvyati 
tathā śrīsatyabhāmāyāṃ lakṣmaṇāyām api kvacit  RUnm 
itthaṃ bhedena bhāvānāṃ sarvagokulasubhruvām 
ātmapakṣavipakṣādibhedāḥ pūrvam udīritāḥ  RUnm 
yā bhāvāntarasambandhāj jāyante vividhā bhidāḥ 
aparā api bhāvānāṃ jñeyās tāḥ prajñayā budhaiḥ  RUnm 
atha anurāgaḥ
sadānubhūtam api yaḥ kuryān navanavaṃ priyam 
rāgo bhavan navanavaḥ so'nurāga itīryate  RUnm 
yathā dānakelikaumudyām 
prapannaḥ panthānaṃ harir asakṛd asmannayanayor
apūrvo'yaṃ pūrvaṃ kvacid api na dṛṣṭo madhurimā 
pratīke'py ekasya sphurati muhur aṅgasya sakhi yā
śriyas tasyāḥ pātuṃ lavam api samarthā na dṛg iyam  RUnm 
yathā vā
ko'yaṃ kṛṣṇa iti vyudasyati dhṛti yas tanvi karṇaṃ viśan
rāgāndhe kim idaṃ sadaiva bhavatī tasyorasi krīḍati 
hāsyaṃ mā kuru mohite tvam adhunā nyastāsya haste mayā
satyaṃ satyam asau dṛgaṅganam agād adyaivaa vidyunnibhaḥ  RUnm 
parasparavaśībhāvaḥ premavaicittyakaṃ tathā 
aprāṇiny api janmāptau lālasābhara unnataḥ 
vipralambhe'sya visphūrtir ity ādyāḥ syur iha kriyāḥ  RUnm 
atra parasparavaśībhāvo yathā
samārambhaṃ pārasparikavijayāya prathan nato
rapūrvā keyaṃ vām aghadamana saṃrambhalaharī 
manohastī bandhas tava yad anayā rāganigaḍai
stvaayāpy asyāḥ premotsavanavaguṇaiś cittahariṇaḥ  RUnm 
premavaicittyasaṃjñas tu vipralambhaḥ sa kathyate  RUnm 
aprāṇiny api janmalālasābharo
yathā dānakelikaumudyām 
tapasyāmah kṣāmodari varayitum venuṣu janur
vareṇyam manyethāḥ sakhi tad akhilānāṃ sujanuṣām 
tapahstomenoccair yad iyam urarñkṛtya muralī
murārāter bimbādharamadhurimānam rasayati  RUnm 
atha vipralambhe visphūrtir yathā
brūyās tvaṃ mathurādhvanīna mathurānāthaṃ tam ity uccakaiḥ
sandeśaṃ vrajasundarī kam api te kācin mayā prāhiṇot 
tatra kṣmāpatipattane yadi gataḥ svacchanda gacchādhunā
kiṃ kliṣṭām api visphuran diśi diśi kliśnāsi hā me sakhīm  RUnm 
atha bhāvaḥ
anurāgaḥ svasaṃvedyadaśāṃ prāpya prakāśitaḥ 
yāvadāśrayavṛttiś ced bhāva ity abhidhīyate  RUnm 
yathā
rādhāyā bhavataś ca cittajatunī svedair vilāpya kramāt
yuñjann adrinikuñjakuñjarapate nirdhūtabhedabhramam 
citrāya svayam anvarañjayad iha brahmāṇḍaharmyodare
bhūyobhir navarāgahiṅgulabharaiḥ śṛṅgārakāruḥ kṛtī  RUnm 
mukundamahiṣīvṛndair apy asāv atidurlabhaḥ 
vrajadevy ekasaṃvedyo mahābhāvākhyayocyate  RUnm 
varāmṛtasvarūpaśrīḥ svaṃ svarūpaṃ mano nayet  RUnm 
sa rūḍhaś cādhirūḍhaś cety ucyate dvividho budhaiḥ  RUnm 
tatra rūḍhaḥ
uddīptā sāttvikā yatra sa rūḍha iti bhaṇyate  RUnm 
nimeṣāsahatāsannajanatāhṛdviloḍanam 
kalpakṣaṇatvaṃ khinnatvaṃ tatsaukhye'py ārtiśaṅkayā  RUnm 
mohādyabhāve'py ātmādisarvavismaraṇaṃ sadā 
kṣaṇasya kalpaetyādyā yatra yogaviyogayoḥ  RUnm 
tatra nimeṣāsahatā
yathā śrīdaśame 
gopyaś ca kṛṣṇam upalabhya cirād abhīṣṭaṃ
yatprekṣaṇe dṛśiṣu pakṣmakṛtaṃ śapanti 
dṛgbhir hṛdīkṛtam alaṃ parirabhya sarvās
tadbhāvam āpur api nityayujāṃ durāpam  RUnm 
āsannajanatāhṛdviloḍanaṃ yathā
sakhyaḥ prokṣya kurūn gurukṣitibhṛtām āghūrṇayantī śiraḥ
svasthā viślathayanty aśeṣaramaṇīr āplāvya sarvaṃ janam 
gopīnām anurāgasindhulaharī satyāntaraṃ vikramai
rākramya stimitāṃ vyadhād api parāṃ vaikuṇṭhakaṇṭhaśriyam  RUnm 
kalpakṣaṇatvam yathā
śarajjyotsnī rāse vidhir ajanirūpāpi nimiṣā
datikṣudrā tāsāṃ yad ajani na tad vismayapadam 
sukhotsekārambhe nimiṣalavakalpām iva daśāṃ
mahākalpākalpāpy ahaha labhate kālakalanā  RUnm 
tatsaukhye'py ārtiśaṅkayā khinnatvam
yathā śrīdaśame 
yat te sujātacaraṇāmburuhaṃ staneṣu
bhītāḥ śanaiḥ priya dadhīmahi karkaśeṣu
tenāṭavīm aṭasi tad vyathate na kiṃ svit
kūrpādibhir bhramati dhīr bhavadāyuṣāṃ naḥ  RUnm 
mohādyabhāve'pi sarvavismaraṇaṃ
yathā ekādaśe 
tā nāvidan mayy anuṣaṅgabaddha
dhiyaḥ svam ātmānam adas tathedam
yathā samādhau munayo'bdhitoye
nadyaḥ praviṣṭā iva nāmarūpe  RUnm 
kṣaṇakalpatā
yathā tatraiva 
tās tāḥ kṣapāḥ preṣṭhatamena nītā
mayaiva vṛndāvanagocareṇa 
kṣaṇārdhavat tāḥ punar aṅga tāsāṃ
hīnā mayā kalpasamā babhūvuḥ  RUnm 
ādyaśabdād iha proktā kṛṣṇāvirbhāvakāritā 
sambhogabhede vispaṣṭaṃ sā purastāt pravakṣyate  RUnm 
atha adhirūḍhaḥ
rūḍhoktebhyo'nubhāvebhyaḥ kām apy āptā viśiṣṭatām 
yatrānubhāvā dṛśyante so'dhirūḍho nigadyate  RUnm 
yathā śivavākyam
lokātīatam ajāṇḍakoṭigam api traikālikaṃ yat sukhaṃ
duḥkhaṃ ceti pṛthag yadi sphuṭam ubhe te gacchataḥ kuṭatām 
naivābhāsatulāṃ śive tad api tat kuṭadvayaṃ rādhikā
premodyatsukhaduḥkhasindhubhavayor vindeta bindvor api  RUnm 
modano mādanaś cāsāv adhirūḍho dvidhocyate  RUnm 
tatra modanaḥ
modanaḥ sa dvayor yatra sāttvikoddīptasauṣṭhavam  RUnm 
yathā lalitamādhave 
ātanvan kalakaṇṭhanādam atulaṃ stambhaśriyojjṛmbhito
bhūyiṣṭhocchaladaṅkuraḥ phalitavān svedāmbumuktāphalaiḥ 
udyadbāṣpamarandabhāgavicalo'py utkampavān vibhramai
rādhāmādhavayor virājati cirād ullāsakalpadrumaḥ  RUnm 
harer yatra sakāntasya vikṣobhabharakāritā 
premorusampadvikhyātakāntātiśayitādayaḥ  RUnm 
rādhikāyūtha evāsau modano na tu sarvataḥ 
yaḥ śrīmān hlādinīśakteḥ suvilāsaḥ priyo varaḥ  RUnm 
tatra sakāntasya hareḥ kṣobhabharakāritā yathā
hanta stambhakarambitā bhuvi kuror bhadrā sarasvaty abhū
dbāṣpaṃ bhāskarajā mumoca tarasā satyābhraman narmadā 
bheje bhīṣmasutā ca varṇavikṛtiṃ gāmbhīryabhāg apy asau
kṛṣṇodanvati rādhikādbhutanadīpremormibhiḥ saṃvṛte  RUnm 
premorusampadvatīvṛndātiśayitvaṃ yathā
advaitād girijāṃ harārdhavapuṣaṃ sakhyāt priyoraḥsthitāṃ
lakṣmīm acyutacittabhṛṅganalinīṃ satyāṃ ca saubhāgyataḥ 
mādhuryān madhureśajīvitasakhīṃ candrāvalīṃ ca kṣipan
paśyāruddha hariṃ prasārya laharīṃ rādhānurāgāmbudhiḥ  RUnm 
modano'yaṃ praviśleṣadaśāyāṃ mohano bhavet 
yasmin virahavaivaśyāt sūddīptā eva sāttvikāḥ  RUnm 
yathā
udyadvepathuvādyamānadaśanā kaṇṭhasthalāntar luṭha
jjalpā gokulamaṇḍalaṃ vidadhatī bāṣpair nadīmātṛkam 
rādhā kaṇṭakitena kaṇṭakiphalaṃ gātreṇa dhikkurvatī
citraṃ tadghanarāgarāśibhir api śvetīkṛtā vartate  RUnm 
atrānubhāvā govinda kāntāśliṣṭe'pi mūrcchanā 
asahyaduḥkhasvīkārād api tatsukhakāmatā  RUnm 
brahmāṇḍakṣobhakāritvaṃ tiraścām api rodanam 
svabhūtair api tatsaṅgatṛṣṇā mṛtyupratiśravāt 
divyonmādādayo'py anye vidvadbhir anukīrtitāḥ  RUnm 
prāyo vṛndāvaneśvaryāṃ mohano'yam udañcati 
samyagvilakṣaṇaṃ yasya kāryaṃ sañcārimohataḥ  RUnm 
tatra kāntāśliṣṭe'pi harau mūrcchākāritvaṃ
yathā padyāvalyām 
ratnacchāyācchuritajaladhau mandire dvārakāyā
rukmiṇyāpi prabalapulakodbhedam āliṅgitasya 
viśvaṃ pāyān masṛṇayamunātīravānīrakuñje
rādhākelīparimalabharadhyānamūrcchā murāreḥ  RUnm 
asahyaduḥkhasvīkārāt tatsukhakāmatā
syān naḥ saukhyaṃ yad api balavad goṣṭham āpte mukunde
yady alpāpi kṣatir udayate tasya māgāt kadāpi 
aprāpte'smin yad api nagarād ārtir ugrā bhaven naḥ
saukhyaṃ tasya sphurati hṛdi cet tatra vāsaṃ karotu  RUnm 
brahmāṇḍakṣobhakāritvaṃ yathā
nāraṃ cukrośa cakraṃ phaṇikulam abhavad vyākulaṃ svedam ūhe
vṛndaṃ vṛndārakāṇāṃ pracuramudam amucann aśru vaikuṇṭhabhājaḥ 
rādhāyāś citram īśa bhramati diśi diśi premaniḥśvāsadhūme
pūrṇānande'py uṣitvā bahir idam abahiś cārtam āsīd ajāṇḍam  RUnm 
yathā vā
aurvastomāt kaṭur api kathaṃ durbalenorasā me
tāpaḥ prauḍho harivirahajaḥ sahyate tan na jāne 
niṣkrāntā ced bhavati hṛdayād yasya dhūmacchaṭāpi
brahmāṇḍānāṃ sakhi kulam api jvālayā jājvalīti  RUnm 
tiraścām api rodanam
yathā padyāvalyām 
yāte dvāravatīpuraṃ muraripau tadvastrasaṃvyānayā
kālindītaṭakuñjavañjulalatām ālāmbya sotkaṇṭhayā 
udgītaṃ gurubāṣpagadgadagalattārasvaraṃ rādhayā
yenāntarjalacāribhir jalacarair apy utkam utkūjitam  RUnm 
mṛtyusvīkārāt svabhūtair api tatsaṅgatṛṣṇā
yathā tatraiva 
pañcatvaṃ tanur etu bhūtanivahāu svāṃśe viśantu sphuṭaṃ
dhātāraṃ praṇipatya hanta śirasā tatrāpi yāce varam 
tadvāpīṣu payas tadīyamukure jyotis tadīyāṅgana
vyomni vyoma tadīyavartmani dharā tattālavṛnte'nilaḥ  RUnm 
atha divyonmādaḥ
etasya mohanākhyasya gatiṃ kāmapy upeyuṣaḥ 
bhramābhā kāpi vaicitrī divyonmāda itīryate  RUnm 
udghūrṇācitrajalpādyās tadbhedā bahavo matāḥ  RUnm 
tatra udghūrṇā
syād vilakṣaṇam udghūrṇā nānāvaivaśyaceṣṭitam  RUnm 
yathā
śayyāṃ kuñjagṛhe kvacid vitanute sā vāsasajjāyitā
nīlābhraṃ dhṛtakhaṇḍitā vyavahṛtiś caṇḍī kvacit tarjati 
āghūrṇatyabhisārasambhramavatī dhvānte kvacid dāruṇe
rādhā te virahodbhramapramathitā dhatte na kāṃ vā daśām  RUnm 
mathurānagaraṃ kṛṣṇe labdhe lalitamādhave 
udghūrṇeyaṃ tṛtīyāṅke rādhāyāḥ sphuṭam īritā  RUnm 
atha citrajalpaḥ
preṣṭhasya suhṛdāloke gūḍharoṣābhijṛmbhitaḥ 
bhūribhāvamayo jalpo yas tīvrotkaṇṭhitāntimaḥ  RUnm 
citrajalpo daśāṅgo'yaṃ prajalpaḥ parijalpitam 
vijalpojjalpasaṃjalpā avajalpo'bhijalpitam 
ājalpaḥ pratijalpaś ca sujalpaś ceti kīrtitāḥ  RUnm 
eṣa bhramaragītākhyo daśame prakaṭīkṛtaḥ  RUnm 
asaṅkhyabhāvavaicitrī camatkṛtisudustaraḥ 
api cec citrajalpo'yaṃ manāk tad api kathyate  RUnm 
tatra prajalpaḥ
asūyerṣyāmadayujā yo'vadhīraṇamudrayā 
priyasyākauśalodgāraḥ prajalpaḥ sa tu kīrtyate  RUnm 
yathā 
madhupa kitavabandho mā spṛśāṅghriṃ sapatnyāḥ
kucavilulitamālākuṅkumaśmaśrubhir naḥ 
vahatu madhupatis tanmāninīnāṃ prasādaṃ
yadusadasi viḍambyaṃ yasya dūtas tvam īdṛk  RUnm 
atha parijalpitam
prabhor nirdayatāśāṭhyacāpalādyupapādanāt 
svavicakṣaṇatāvyaktir bhaṅgyā syāt parijalpitam  RUnm 
yathā 
sakṛd adharasudhāṃ svāṃ mohinīṃ pāyayitvā
sumanasa iva sadyas tatyaje'smān bhavādṛk 
paricarati kathaṃ tatpādapadmaṃ nu padmā
hy api bata hṛtacetā hy uttamaḥślokajalpaiḥ  RUnm 
atha vijalpaḥ
vyaktayāsūyayā gūḍhamānamudrāntarālayā 
aghadviṣi kaṭākṣoktir vijalpo viduṣāṃ mataḥ  RUnm 
yathā 
kim iha bahu ṣaḍaṅghre gāyasi tvaṃ yadūnām
adhipatim agṛhāṇām agrato naḥ purāṇam 
vijayasakhasakhīnāṃ gīyatāṃ tatprasaṅgaḥ
kṣapitakucarujas te kalpayantīṣṭam iṣṭāḥ  RUnm 
atha ujjalpaḥ
hareḥ kuhakatākhyānaṃ garvagarbhitayerṣyayā 
sāsūyaś ca tadākṣepo dhīrair ujjalpa īryate  RUnm 
yathā 
divi bhuvi ca rasāyāṃ kāḥ striyas taddurāpāḥ
kapaṭarucirahāsabhrūvijṛmbhasya yāḥ syuḥ 
caraṇaraja upāste yasya bhūtir vayaṃ kā
api ca kṛpaṇapakṣe hy uttamaḥślokaśabdaḥ  RUnm 
atha saṃjalpaḥ
solluṇṭhayā gahanayā kayāpy ākṣepamudrayā 
tasyākṛtajñatādyuktiḥ saṃjalpaḥ kathito budhaiḥ  RUnm 
yathā 
visṛja śirasi pādaṃ vedmy ahaṃ cāṭukārair
anunayaviduṣas te'bhyetya dautyair mukundāt 
svakṛta iha visṛṣṭāpatyapatyanyalokā
vyasṛjad akṛtacetāḥ kiṃ nu sandheyam asmin  RUnm 
atha avajalpaḥ
harau kāṭhinyakāmitvadhaurtyād āsaktyayogyatā 
yatra serṣyaṃ bhiyevoktā so'vajalpaḥ satāṃ mataḥ  RUnm 
yathā 
mṛgayur iva kapīndraṃ vivyadhe lubdhadharmā
striyam akṛta virūpāṃ strījitaḥ kāmayānām 
balim api balim attvāveṣṭayad dhvāṅkṣavad yas
tad alam asitasakhyair dustyajas tatkathārthaḥ  RUnm 
atha abhijalpitam
bhaṅgyā tyāgaucitī tasya khagānām api khedanāt 
yatra sānuśayaṃ proktā tad bhaved abhijalpitam  RUnm 
yathā 
yadanucaritalīlākarṇapīyūṣavipruṭ
sakṛdadanavidhūtadvandvadharmā vinaṣṭāḥ 
sapadi gṛhakuṭumbaṃ dīnam utsṛjya dīnā
bahava iha vihaṅgā bhikṣucaryāṃ caranti  RUnm 
atha ājalpaḥ
jaihmyaṃ tasyārtidatvaṃ ca nirvedād yatra kīrtitam 
bhaṅyānyasukhadatvaṃ ca sa ājalpa udīritaḥ  RUnm 
yathā 
vayam ṛtam iva jihmavyāhṛtaṃ śraddadhānāḥ
kulikarutam ivājñāḥ kṛṣṇavadhvo hariṇyaḥ
dadṛśur asakṛd etat tannakhasparśatīvra
smararuja upamantrin bhaṇyatām anyavārtā  RUnm 
atha pratijalpaḥ
dustyajadvandvabhāve'smin prāptir nārhety anuddhatam 
dūtasammānanenoktaṃ yatra sa pratijalpakaḥ  RUnm 
yathā 
priyasakha punar āgāḥ preyasā preṣitaḥ kiṃ
varaya kim anurundhe mānanīyo'si me'ṅga 
nayasi katham ihāsmān dustyajadvandvapārśvaṃ
satatam urasi saumya śrīr vadhūḥ sākam āste  RUnm 
atha sujalpaḥ
yatrārjavāt sagāmbhīryaṃ sadainyaṃ sahacāpalam 
sotkaṇṭhaṃ ca hariḥ pṛṣṭaḥ sa sujalpo nigadyate  RUnm 
yathā 
api bata madhupuryām āryaputro'dhunāste
smarati sa pitṛgehān saumya bandhūṃś ca gopān 
kvacid api sa kathāṃ naḥ kiṅkarīṇāṃ gṛṇīte
bhujam agurusugandhaṃ mūrdhny adhāsyat kadā nu  RUnm 
atha mādanaḥ
sarvabhāvodgamollāsī mādano'yaṃ parāt paraḥ 
rājate hlādinīsāro rādhāyām eva yaḥ sadā  RUnm 
yathā
āsṛṣṭer akṣayiṣṇuṃ hṛdayavidhumaṇidrāvaṇaṃ vakrimāṇaṃ
pūrṇatve'py udvahantaṃ nijarucighaṭayā sādhvasaṃ dhvaṃsayantam 
tanvānaṃ śaṃ pradoṣe dhṛtanavanavatāsampadaṃ mādanatvā
dadvaitaṃ naumi rādhādanujavijayinor adbhutaṃ bhāvacandram
atrerṣyāyā ayogye'pi prabalerṣyāvidhāyitā 
sadābhoge'pi tadgandhamātrādhārastavādayaḥ  RUnm 
atha ayogye'pīrṣyā
yathā dānakelikaumudyām 
viśuddhābhiḥ sārdhaṃ vrajahariṇanetrābhir aniśaṃ
tvam addhā vidveṣaṃ kim iti vanamāle racayasi 
tṛṇīkurvaty asmān vapur agharipor āśikham idaṃ
pariṣvajyāpāda mahati hṛdaye yā viharasi  RUnm 
sadābhoge'pi tadgandhamātrādhārastutir
yathā śrīdaśame 
pūrṇāḥ pulindya urugāyapadābjarāga
śrīkuṅkumena dayitāstanamaṇḍitena 
taddarśanasmararujas tṛṇarūṣitena
limpantya ānanakuceṣu juhus tadādhim  RUnm 
yathā vā
duṣkaraṃ kataradāli mālatī
komaleyam akarot tapaḥ purā 
hanta goṣṭhapatinandanopamaṃ
yā tamālam amalopagūhate  RUnm 
yoga eva bhaved eṣa vicitraḥ ko'pi mādanaḥ 
yadvilāsā virājante nityalīlāḥ sahasradhā  RUnm 
mādanasya gatiḥ suṣṭhu madanasyeva durgamā 
na nirvaktuṃ bhavec chakyā tenāsau munināpy alam  RUnm 
kiṃ ca
rāgānurāgatām ādau snehaḥ prāpyaiva satvaram 
mānatvaṃ praṇayatvaṃ ca kvacit paścāt prapadyate  RUnm 
ataevātra śāstreṣu śrūyate rādhikādiṣu 
pūrvarāgaprasaṅge'pi prakaṭaṃ rāgalakṣaṇam  RUnm 
sphuranti vrajadevīṣu parā bhāvabhidāś ca yāḥ 
tās tarkāygocaratyā na samyag iha varṇitāḥ  RUnm 
sādhāraṇyāṃ ratāv eva dhūmāyitatayā matāḥ 
jvalitās tu ratipremṇor dīptāḥ snehādipañcasu 
rūḍhe bhāve tathoddīptāḥ sudīptā mohanādiṣu  RUnm 
iyaṃ prāyikatā kintu śreṣṭhamadhyādibhārataḥ 
deśakālajanādīnāṃ kvāpy eṣāṃ syād viparyayam  RUnm 
ādyā premāntimāṃ tatrānurāgāntāṃ samañjasā 
ratir bhāvāntimāṃ sīmāṃ samarthaiva prapadyante  RUnm 
ratir narmavayasyānām anurāgāntimāṃ sthitim 
teṣv eva subalādīnāṃ bhāvāntām eva gacchati  RUnm 
iti śrīśrīujjvalanīlamaṇau
sthāyibhāvaprakaraṇam  
atha śṛṅgārabhedaprakaraṇam
sa vipralambhaḥ sambhoga iti dvedhojjvalo mataḥ  RUnm 
tatra vipralambhaḥ
yūnor ayuktayor bhāvo yuktayor vā tayor mithaḥ 
abhīṣṭāliṅganādīnām anavāptau prakṛṣyate 
sa vipralambho vijñeyaḥ sambhogonnatikārakaḥ  RUnm 
tathā coktam
na vinā vipralambhena sambhogaḥ puṣṭim aśnute 
kāṣāyite hi vastrādau bhūyān evābhivardhate  RUnm 
pūrvarāgas tathā mānaḥ premavaicittyam ity api 
pravāsaś ceti kathito vipralambhaś caturvidhaḥ  RUnm 
tatra pūrvarāgaḥ
ratir yā saṅgamāt pūrvaṃ darśanaśravaṇādijā 
tayor unmīlati prājñaiḥ pūrvarāgaḥ sa ucyate  RUnm 
tatra darśanāt
sākṣāt kṛṣṇasya citre ca syāt svapnādau ca darśanam  RUnm 
tatra sākṣāt
yathā padyāvalyām 
indīvarodarasahodarameduraśrīr
vāso dravatkanakavṛndanibhaṃ dadhānaḥ 
āmuktamauktikamanoharahāravakṣāḥ
ko'yaṃ yuvā jagadanaṅgamayaṃ karoti  RUnm 
citre yathā vidagdhamādhave 
śiśiraya dṛśau dṛṣṭvā divyaṃ kiśoram itīkṣitaḥ
parijalpanagirāṃ viśrambhāt tvaṃ vilāsaphalāṅkitaḥ 
śiva śiva kathaṃ jānīmas tvām avakradhiyo vayaṃ
niviḍabaḍavāvahnijvālākalāpavikāsinam  RUnm 
svapne yathā
svapne dṛṣṭvā sahacari saritkāsarī śyāmanīrā
tīre tasyāḥ kvaṇitamadhupā mādhavaīkuñjaśālā 
tasyāṃ kāntaṃ kapiśajaghano dhvāntarāśiḥ śarīrī
citraṃ candrāvalim api sa māṃ pātum icchann arautsīt  RUnm 
atha śravaṇam
vandidūtīsakhīvaktrād gītādeś ca śrutir bhavet  RUnm 
tato vandivaktrāt yathā
paṭhati magadharājanirjayārthāṃ
sakhi virudāvalim atra vandivarye 
vada katham iva lakṣmaṇe tanute
pulakakulena vilakṣaṇā kilāsīt  RUnm 
dūtīvaktrāt yathā
āviṣkṛte tava mukunda mayā prasaṅge
tārāvalī pulakitāṅgalatā natākṣī 
śuśrūṣur apy alaghugadgadaruddhakaṇṭhī
praṣṭuṃ tavākṣamata sā na kathāviśeṣam  RUnm 
sakhīvaktrāt yathā
yāvad unmadacakoralocanā
manmukhāt tava kathām upāśṛṇot 
tāvad añcati dinaṃ dinaṃ sakhī
kṛṣṇa śārad anadīrya tānavam  RUnm 
gītāt yathā
nayane praṇayann udaśruṇī
mama sadyaḥ sadasi kṣitīśituḥ 
upavīṇayati pravīṇadhīḥ
kam udaśruḥ sakhi vaiṇiko muniḥ  RUnm 
puroktā ye'bhiyogādyā hetavo ratijanmani 
atra te pūrvarāge'pi jñeyā dhīrair yathocitam  RUnm 
api mādhavarāgasya prāthamye sambhavaty api 
ādau rāge mṛgākṣīṇāṃ prokte syāc cārutādhikā  RUnm 
atra sañcāriṇo vyādhiḥ śaṅkāsūyā śramaḥ klamaḥ 
nirvedautsukyadainyāni cintānidrāprabodhanam  RUnm 
viṣādo jaḍatonmado mohamṛtyādayaḥ smṛtāḥ 
prauḍhaḥ samañjasaḥ sādhāraṇaś ceti sa tu tridhā  RUnm 
tatra prauḍhaḥ
samarthaaratirūpas tu prauḍha ity abhidhīyate 
lālasādir iha prauḍhe maraṇāntā daśā bhavet 
tattatsañcāribhāvānām utkaṭatvād anekadhā  RUnm 
tathāpi prāktanair asya daśāvasthā samāsataḥ 
proktās tadanurodhena tāsāṃ lakṣaṇam ucyate  RUnm 
lālasodvegajāgaryās tānavaṃ jaḍimātra tu 
vaiyagryaṃ vyādhir unmādo moho mṛtyur daśā daśa  RUnm 
prauḍhatvāt pūrvarāgasya prauḍhāḥ sarvā daśā api  RUnm 
tatra lālasaḥ
abhīṣṭalipsayā gāḍhagṛdhnutā lālaso mataḥ 
atrautsukyaṃ capalatā ghūrṇāśvāsādayas tathā  RUnm 
yathā
tvam avasitān niṣkrāmantī punaḥ praviśanty asau
jhaṭiti ghaṭikāmadhye vārāñchataṃ vrajasīmani 
agaṇitagurutrāsā śvāsān vimucya vimucya kiṃ
kṣipasi bahuśo nīpāraṇye kiśori dṛśor dvayam  RUnm 
yathā vā vidagdhamādhave 
dūrād apy anuṣaṅgataḥ śrutim ite tvannāmadheyākṣare
sonmādaṃ madirekṣaṇā viruvatī dhatte muhur vepathum 
āḥ kiṃ vā kathanīyam anyadasite daivād varāmbhodhare
dṛṣṭe taṃ parirabdhum utsukamatiḥ pakṣadvayīm icchati  RUnm 
atha udvegaḥ
udvego manasaḥ kampas tatra niḥśvāsacāpale 
stambhaś cintāśruvaivarṇyasvedādaya udīritāḥ  RUnm 
yathā vidagdhamādhave 
cintāsantatir adya kṛntati sakhi svāntasya kiṃ te dhṛtiṃ
kiṃvā siñcati tāmram ambaram atisvedāmbhasāṃ ḍambaraḥ 
kampaś campakagauri lumpati vapuḥsthairyaṃ kathaṃ vā balāt
tathyaṃ brūhi na maṅgalā parijane saṅgopanāṅgīkṛtiḥ  RUnm 
atha jāgaryā
nidrākṣayas tu jāgaryā stambhaśoṣagadādikṛt  RUnm 
yathā
śyāmaṃ kañcana kāñcanojjvalapaṭaṃ sandarśya nidrā kṣaṇaṃ
mām ājanma sakhī vimucya calitā ruṣṭeva nāvartate 
cintāṃ prohya sakhi prapañcaya matiṃ tasyās tvam āvartane
nānyaḥ svāpnikataskaropaharaṇe śakto janas tāṃ vinā  RUnm 
atha tānavam
tānavaṃ kṛśatā gātre daurbalyabhramaṇādikṛt  RUnm 
yathā
cyute valayasañcaye prabalariktatādūṣaṇa
vyayāya nihitormikāvalir api skhalaty añjasā 
niśamya muralīkalaṃ sakhi sakṛd viśākhe tanu
stavāsitacaturdaśīśaśikalā kṛśatvaṃ yayau  RUnm 
kaiścit tu tānavasthāne vilāpaḥ paripaṭhyate  RUnm 
yathā
atrāsīn navanīpabhūruhataṭe kurvan vihāraṃ hari
ścakre tāṇḍavam atra mitrasahitaś caṇḍāṃśujārodhasi 
paśyantī latikāntare kṣaṇam ahaṃ vyagrā nilīya sthitaṃ
sakhyaḥ kiṃ kathayāmi dagdhavidhinā kṣiptāsmi dāvopari  RUnm 
atha jaḍimā
iṣṭāniṣṭāparijñānaṃ yatra praśneṣv anuttaram 
darśanaśravaṇābhāvo jaḍimā so'bhidhīyate 
atrākāṇḍe'pi huṅkārastambhaśvāsabhramādayaḥ  RUnm 
yathā
akāṇḍe huṅkāraṃ racayasi śṛṇoṣi priyasakhī
kulānāṃ nālāpaṃ dṛtir iva muhur niḥśvasiṣi ca 
tataḥ śaṅke paṅkeruhamukhi yayau vaiṇavakalā
madhulī te pāli śruticaṣakayoḥ prāghūṇikatām  RUnm 
atha vaiyāgryam
vaiyāgryaṃ bhāvagāmbhīryavikṣobhāsahatocyate 
tatrāvivekanirvedakhedāsūyādayo matāḥ  RUnm 
yathā vidagdhamādhave 
pratyāhṛtya muniḥ kṣaṇaṃ viṣayato yasmin mano dhitsate
bālāsau viṣayeṣu dhitsati tataḥ pratyāharantī manaḥ 
yasya sphūrtilavāya hanta hṛdaye yogī sumutkaṇṭhate
mugdheyaṃ kila tasya paśya hṛdayān niṣkrāntim ākāṅkṣati  RUnm 
atha vyādhiḥ
abhīṣṭālābhato vyādhiḥ pāṇḍimottāpalakṣaṇaḥ 
atra śītaspṛhāmohaniḥśvāsapatanādayaḥ  RUnm 
yathā
davadamanatayā niśamya bhadrā
madanadavajvalitā dadhe hṛdi tvām 
dviguṇitadavathuvyathāvidagdhā
murahara bhasmamayīva pāṇḍurāsīt  RUnm 
atha unmādaḥ
sarvāvasthāsu sarvatra tanmanaskatayā sadā 
atasmiṃs tu tad iti bhrāntir unmāda iti kīrtyate 
atreṣṭadveṣaniḥśvāsanimeṣavirahādayaḥ  RUnm 
yathā vidagdhamādhave 
vitanvānas tanvā marakatarucīnāṃ rucivatāṃ
paṭān niṣkrānto'bhūd dhṛtaśikhaṇḍo navayuvā 
bhruvaṃ tena kṣiptvā kim api hasatonmāditamateḥ
śaśī vṛtto vahniḥ param ahaha vahnir mama śaśī  RUnm 
atha mohaḥ
moho vicittatā prokto naiścalyapatanādikṛt  RUnm 
yathā
nāsāśvāsaparāṅmukhī vighaṭite dṛṣṭī snuṣāyāḥ kathaṃ
hā dhik kṛṣṇatilān mamārpaya kare kuryām apāmārjanam 
ity ārohati karṇayoḥ parisaraṃ kṛṣṇeti karṇadvaye
kampenācyuta tatra sūtritavatī tvām eva hetuṃ sakhī  RUnm 
atha mṛtyuḥ
tais taiḥ kṛtaiḥ pratīkārair yadi na syāt samāgamaḥ 
kandarpabāṇakadanāt tatra syān maraṇodyamaḥ  RUnm 
tatra svapriyavastūnāṃ vayasyāsu samarpaṇam 
bhṛṅgamandānilajyotsnākadambānubhavādayaḥ  RUnm 
yathā
rādhā rodhasi ropitāṃ mukulinīm āliṅgya mallīlatāṃ
hāraṃ hīramayaṃ samarpya lalitāhaste praśastaśriyam 
mūrcchām āpnuvatī praviśya madhupair gītāṃ kadambāṭavīṃ
nāma vyāharatā hareḥ priyasakhīvṛndena sandhukṣitā  RUnm 
yathā vā vidagdhamādhave 
akāruṇyaḥ kṛṣṇo yadi mayi tavāgaḥ katham idaṃ
mudhā mā rodīr me kuru param imām uttarakṛtim 
tamālasya skandhe vinihitabhujavallarir iyaṃ
yathā vṛndāraṇye ciram avicalā tiṣṭhati tanuḥ  RUnm 
atha samañjasaḥ
bhavet samañjasaratisvarūpo'yaṃ samañjasaḥ  RUnm 
atrābhilāṣacintāsmṛtiguṇasaṅkīrtanodvegāḥ 
savilāpā unmādavyādhijaḍatā mṛtiś ca tāḥ kramaśaḥ  RUnm 
tatra abhilāṣaḥ
vyavasāyo'bhilāṣaḥ syāt priyasaṅgam alipsayā 
svamaṇḍanāntikaprāptirāgaprakaṭanādikṛt  RUnm 
yathā
yad iha sakhi subhadrāsakhyam ākhyāya dhūrte
vrajasi pitur agārād devekīmandirāya 
racayasi bata satye maṇḍane ca prayatnaṃ
sphuṭam ajani tad antar vastu gūḍhaṃ tavādya  RUnm 
atha cintā
abhīṣṭāvāptyupāyānāṃ dhyānaṃ cintā prakīrtitā 
śayyāvivṛttiniḥśvāsanirlakṣaprekṣaṇādikṛt  RUnm 
yathā
niḥśvāsas te kamalavadane mlāpayatyoṣṭhabimbaṃ
śayyāyāṃ ca kraśimakalitā ceṣṭate dehayaṣṭiḥ 
dvandvaṃ cākṣṇor vikirati ciraṃ rukmiṇi śyāma ambho
na śvobhāviny upayamavidhau śobhate vikriyeyam  RUnm 
atha smṛtiḥ
anubhūtapriyādīnām arthānāṃ cintanaṃ smṛtiḥ 
atra kampāṅgavaivaśyabāṣpaniḥśvasitādayaḥ  RUnm 
yathā
plutaṃ pureṇāpāṃ nayanakamaladvandvam abhito
dhṛtotkampaṃ sātrājiti kucarathāṅgadvayam api 
ślathārambhaṃ caitad bhujavisalayugaṃ tat tava mana
staḍāge'smin kṛṣṇadviradapatir antar viharati  RUnm 
atha guṇakīrtanam
saundaryādiguṇaślāghā guṇakīrtanam ucyate 
atra vepathuromāñcakaṇṭhagadgadikādayaḥ  RUnm 
yathā
yāntyas tṛṣṇāpi yuvatayo yeṣu ghūrṇāṃ bhajante
yāny ācamya svayam api bhavān romaharṣaṃ prayāti 
gandhaṃ teṣāṃ tava madhupate rūpasampanmadhūnāṃ
dūre vindan mama na hi dhṛtiḥ cittabhṛṅgas tanoti  RUnm 
ṣaḍudvegādayaḥ pūrvaṃ prauḍhe tasminn udāhṛtāḥ 
sāmañjasyād rater atra kintu tāḥ syur yathocitam  RUnm 
atha sādhāraṇaḥ
sādhāraṇaratiprāyaḥ sādhāraṇa itīritaḥ 
atra proktā vilāpāntāḥ ṣaḍdaśāntāś ca komalāḥ  RUnm 
atha abhilāṣo
yathā prathamaskandhe 
etāḥ paraṃ strītvam apāstapeśalaṃ
nirastaśaucaṃ bata sādhu kurvate 
yāsāṃ gṛhāt puṣkaralocanaḥ patir
na jātv apaity āhṛtibhir hṛdi spṛśan  RUnm 
cintādīnāṃ tathānyāsām ūhyā dhīrair udāhṛtiḥ  RUnm 
pūrvarāge prahīyeta kāmalekhasragādikam 
vayasyādikareṇātra kṛṣṇenāsya ca kāntayā  RUnm 
tatra kāmalekhaḥ
sa lekhaḥ kāmalekhaḥ syāt yaḥ svapremaprakāśakaḥ 
yuvatyā yūni yūnā ca yuvatyāṃ saṃprahīyate  RUnm 
nirakṣaraḥ sākṣaraś ca kāmalekho dvidhā bhavet  RUnm 
tatra nirakṣaraḥ
suraktapallavamayaś candrārdhādinakhāṅkabhāk 
varṇavinyāsarahito bhaved eṣa nirakṣaraḥ  RUnm 
yathā
kisalayaśikhare viśākhikāyā
nakharaśikhālikhito'yam ardhacandraḥ 
dadhad iha madanārdhacandrabhāvaṃ
hṛdi mama hanta kathaṃ haṭhād viveśa  RUnm 
atha sākṣaram
gāthāmayī lipir yatra svahastāṅkaiṣa sākṣaraḥ  RUnm 
yathā jagannāthavallabhe
suiraṃ vijjhasi hiaaṃ lambhai maaṇo kkhu dujjasaḥ baliaṃ 
dīsasi saaladisāsuṃ dīsai maaṇo ṇa kuttābi  RUnm 
suciraṃ bidhyasi hṛdayaṃ labhate madanaḥ khalu duryaśo balīyaḥ 
dṛśyase sakaladiśāsu dṛśyate madano na kutrāpi 
bandho'bjatantunā rāgaḥ kiṃ vā kastūrikāmasī 
pṛthupuṣpadalaṃ patraḥ mudrākṛt kuṅkumair iha  RUnm 
atha mālyārpaṇam
suśliṣṭāṃ nijaśilpakauśalabharavyāhāriṇīm adbhutāṃ
goṣṭhādhīśvaranandanaṃ srajam imāṃ tubhyaṃ sakhi prāhiṇot 
ity ākarṇya giraṃ saroruhadṛśaḥ svedodabindūcchalā
daṅgebhyaḥ kuladharmadhairyam abhitaḥ śaṅke bahir niryayau  RUnm 
kecit tu
nayanaprītiḥ prathamaṃ cintāsaṅgas tato'tha saṅkalpaḥ 
nidrācchedas tanutā viṣayanivṛttis trapānāpa 
unmādo mūrcchā mṛtir ity etāḥ smaradaśā daśaiva syuḥ  RUnm 
ity ācakṣate 
evaṃ krameṇa vijñeyaḥ pūrvarāgo harer api 
nidarśanāya tatraikam udāharaṇam ucyate  RUnm 
yathā
upāraṃsīd vaṃśīkalaparimalollāsarabhasā
dvisasmāra sphārāṃ vividhakusumākalparacanām 
jahau kṛṣṇas tṛṣṇāṃ sahacaracamūcārucarite
sakhi tvadbhrūvyālīculukitacalaccittapavanaḥ  RUnm 
iti pūrvarāgaḥ 
atha mānaḥ
dampatyor bhāva ekatra sator apy anuraktayoḥ 
svābhīṣṭāśleṣavīkṣādinirodhī māna ucyate  RUnm 
sañcāriṇo'tra nirvedaśaṅkāmarṣāḥ sacāpalāḥ 
garvāsūyāvahitthāś ca glāniś cintādayo'py amī  RUnm 
ahetor neti nety uker hetor yan māna ucyate 
asya praṇaya eva syān mānasya padam uttamam  RUnm 
tatra sahetuḥ
hetur īrṣyāvipakṣāder vaiśiṣṭye preyasā kṛte 
bhāvaḥ praṇayamukhyo'yam īṛṣāmānatvam ṛcchati  RUnm 
tathā coktam śṛṅgāratilaka 
snehaṃ vinā bhayaṃ na syān nerṣyā ca praṇayaṃ vinā 
tasmān mānaprakāro'yaṃ dvayoḥ premaprakāśakaḥ  RUnm 
ataeva harivaṃśe  
ruṣitām iva tāṃ devīṃ snehāt saṅkalpayann iva 
bhītabhīto'tiśanakair viveśa yadunandanaḥ  RUnm 
rūpayauvanasampannā svasaubhāgyena garvitā 
abhimānavatī devī śrutvaiverṣyāvaśaṃ gatā  RUnm 
iti 
tatrāpi ca susakhyādi hṛdi yasyā virājate 
tasyā vipakṣavaiśiṣṭye na syād eva sahiṣṇutā  RUnm 
ataḥ satyāṃ vinānyāsāṃ susakhyāder abhāvataḥ 
śrute'pi pārijātasya dāne māno na cābhavat  RUnm 
śrutaṃ cānumitaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ tadvaiśiṣṭyaṃ tridhā matam  RUnm 
atha śravaṇam
śravaṇaṃ tu priyasakhīśukādīnāṃ mukhād bhavet  RUnm 
tatra sakhīmukhāt yathā
śaśimukhi mṛṣā jalpaṃ śrutvā kaṭhorasakhīmukhāt
praṇayini harau mā viśrambhaṃ kṛthāḥ śithilaṃ vṛthā 
parihara manaḥklāntiṃ devi prasīda manorame
tava mukham anālocya preyān vane'dya viśīryati  RUnm 
yathā vā
ahaha gahanā keyaṃ vārtā śrutau patitādya me
viditam anṛtaṃ hāsyād brūṣe vimuñca kadarthanām 
sahacari kuto jīvaty asmin jane'pi janārdano
dyutaru kusumaṃ tasyai hā dhik kṛtī vitariṣyati  RUnm 
śukamukhā yathā
āste kācid dayitakalahā krūracetāḥ sakhī te
kīro vanyaḥ sphuṭam iha yayā śyāmale pāṭhito'sti 
atha vyarthe vihagalapite suṣṭhu viśrambhamāṇā
mānārambhe na kuru hṛdayaṃ kātaro'smi prasīda  RUnm 
anumitiḥ
bhogāṅkagotraskhalanasvapnair anumitis tridhā  RUnm 
atra bhogāṅkaḥ
bhogāṅko dṛśyate gātre vipakṣasya priyasya ca  RUnm 
tatra vipakṣagātre bhogāṅkadarśanaṃ yathā
kālindītaṭadhūrta cāṭubhir alaṃ nidrātu candrāvalī
khinnākṣī kṣaṇamaṅganād apasara kruddhāsti vṛddhā gṛhe 
kiñcid bimbitadhātupatramakarīcitreṇa tatrādhunā
sarvā te lalitā lalāṭaphalakenodghāṭitā cāturī  RUnm 
priyagātre bhogāṅkadarśanaṃ
yathā vidagdhamādhave 
muktāntarnimiṣaṃ madīyapadavīm udvīkṣamāṇasya
jāne keśarareṇubhir nipatitaiḥ śoṇīkṛte locane 
śītaiḥ kānanavāyubhir viracito bimbādhare ca vraṇaḥ
saṅkocaṃ tyaja deva daivahatayā na tvaṃ mayā dūṣyase  RUnm 
tatra gotraskhalanam
vipakṣasaṃjñayāhvānam īrṣyātiśayakāraṇam 
āsāṃ tu gotraskhalanaṃ duḥkhadaṃ maraṇād api  RUnm 
tena yathā bilvamaṅgale
rādhāmohanamandirād upagataś candrāvalīm ūcivān
rādhe kṣemam iheti tasya vacanaṃ śrutvāha candrāvalī 
kaṃsa kṣemam aye vimugdhahṛdaye kaṃsaḥ kva dṛṣṭas tvayā
rādhā kveti vilajjito natamukhaḥ smero hariḥ pātu vaḥ  RUnm 
yathā vā
ahaha vilasaty agre candrāvalī vimaladyutiḥ
kitava kalitā tārā sātra tvayā kva nu ṣoḍaśī 
timiramalinākāra kṣipraṃ vrajāruṇamaṇḍalā
mama sahacarī yāvanmanyudyutiṃ na vimuñcati  RUnm 
atha svapnaḥ
harer vidūṣakasyāpi svapnaḥ svapnāyitaṃ mataḥ  RUnm 
tatra hareḥ svapnāyitam yathā
śape tubhyaṃ rādhe tvam asi hṛdaye tvaṃ mama bahi
stvam agre tvaṃ pṛṣṭhe tvam iha bhavane tvaṃ girivane 
iti svapne jalpaṃ niśi niśamayantī madhuripo
rabhūt talpe candrāvalir atha parāvartitamukhī  RUnm 
vidūṣakasya yathā
avañci caṭupāṭavair aghabhidādya padmāsakhī
tatas tvaraya rādhikāṃ kim iti mādhavi dhyāyasi 
niśamya madhumaṅgalād iti giraṃ puraḥ svapnajāṃ
vidūnavadanā sakhi jvalati paśya candrāvalī  RUnm 
atha darśanam yathā
mithyā mā vada kandare sama sakhīṃ hitvā tvam ekākinīṃ
niṣkrāntaḥ pṛthusambhrameṇa kim api prakhyāpayan kaitavam 
dūrāt kiñcid añcitena rasanāśabdena sātaṅkayā
niṣkramyātha tayā śaṭhendra puline dṛṣṭo'si rādhāsakhaḥ  RUnm 
yathā vā
sahacari parigumphya prātar evārpitāsīd
brajapatisutakaṇṭhe yā mayotkaṇṭhayādya 
api hṛdi lalitāyās tasthuṣī hanta hṛn me
dahati dahanadīptiḥ paśya guñjāvalī sā  RUnm 
atha nirhetuḥ
akāraṇād dvayor eva kāraṇābhāsatas tathā 
prodyan praṇaya evāyaṃ vrajen nirhetumānatām  RUnm 
ādyaṃ mānaṃ parīṇāmaṃ praṇayasya jagur budhāḥ 
dvitīyaṃ punar asyaiva vilāsabharavaibhavam 
budhaiḥ praṇayamānākhyaṃ eṣa eva prakīrtitaḥ  RUnm 
tathā coktam sarasvatīkaṇṭhābharaṇe 
aher iva gatiḥ premṇaḥ svabhāvakuṭilā bhavet 
ato hetor ahetoś ca yūnor māna udañcati  RUnm 
avahitthādayo hy atra vijñeyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ  RUnm 
tatra kṛṣṇasya yathā
avyaktasmitadṛṣṭim arpaya puraḥ svalpo'pi mantur na me
patyur vañcanapāṭavād vrajapate jyotsnīniśārdhaṃ yayau 
śubhrālaṅkṛtibhir drutaṃ pathi mayā dūraṃ tataḥ prasthite
sāndrā cāndram arundha bimbam acirād ākasmikī kālikā  RUnm 
yathā vā
puṣpebhyaḥ spṛhayā vilambitavatīm ālokya mām unmanāḥ
kaṃsāriḥ sakhi lambitānanaśaśī tūṣṇīṃ nikuñje sthitaḥ 
ātaṅkena mayā tadaṅghrinakhare kṣipte prasūnāñjalau
tasyālīkaruṣā bhruvaṃ vibhujato'py āvirbabhūva smitam  RUnm 
kṛṣṇapriyāyāḥ
yathā uddhavasandeśe 
tiṣṭhan goṣṭhāṅgaṇabhuvi muhurlocanāntaṃ vidhatte
jātotkaṇṭhastava sakhi Harirdehalīvedikāyām 
mithyāmānonnatikavalite kiṃ gavākṣārpitākṣī
svāntam hanta glapayasi bahiḥ prīṇaya prāṇanātham  RUnm 
yathā vā
aham iha vicinomi tvadgiraiva prasūnaṃ
kathaya katham akāṇḍe caṇḍi vācaṃ yamāsi 
viditam upadhinālaṃ rādhike śādhi kena
priyasakhi kusumena śrotram uttaṃsayāmi  RUnm 
dvayor eva yugapad yathā
kuñje tuṣṇīm asi nataśirāḥ kiṃ cirāt tvaṃ murāre
kiṃ vā śyāme tvam api vimukhī maunamudrāṃ tanoṣi 
jñātaṃ jñātaṃ smitavimuṣite kāpi vāmāsti yogyā
krīḍāvāde balavati yayā na dvayor eva bhaṅgaḥ  RUnm 
yathā vā
kuñjadvāri niviṣṭayos taraṇijātīre dvayor eva nau
tatrānyonyam apaśyatoḥ sakhi mudhā nirbandhataḥ klāntayoḥ 
haste drāg atha dāḍimīphalam abhinyaste mayā nistalaṃ
rādhām udbhidurasmitāṃ parihasan phullāṅgam āliṅgiṣam  RUnm 
nirhetukaḥ svayaṃ śāmyet svayaṃgrāhasmitāvidhiḥ  RUnm 
yathā
roṣas tavābhūd yadi rādhike'dhika
stathāstu gaṇḍaḥ katham ucchvasity asau 
svanarmaṇetthaṃ durapahnavasmitāṃ
priyām acumbat paśupendranandanaḥ  RUnm 
hetur yas tu śamaṃ yathāyogyaṃ prakalpitaiḥ 
sāmabhedakriyādānanatyupekṣārasāntaraiḥ  RUnm 
mānopaśamanasyāṅkā bāṣpamokṣasmitādayaḥ  RUnm 
tatra sāma
priyavākyasya racanaṃ yat tu tat sāma gīyate  RUnm 
yathā
jātaṃ sundari tathaym eva pṛthunā rādhe'parādhena me
kintu svārasiko mamātra śaraṇaṃ snehas tvadīyo balī 
ity ākarṇya giraṃ harer natamukhī bāṣpāmbhasāṃ dhārayā
sānaṅgotsavaraṅgamaṅgalaghaṭo pūrṇāvakārṣīt kucau  RUnm 
atha bhedaḥ
bhedo dvidhā svayaṃ bhaṅgyā svamāhātmyaprakāśanam 
sakhyādibhir upālambhaprayogaś ceti kīrtyate  RUnm 
tatra bhaṅgyā svamāhātmyaprakāśanaṃ
yathā vidagdhamādhave 
cañcanmīnavilocanāsi kamaṭhotakṛṣṭastanī saṅgatā
kroṅena sphuratā tavāyam adharaḥ prahlādasaṃvardhanaḥ 
madhyo'sau balibandhano mukharucā rāmās tvayā nirjitā
labdhā śrīghanatādya mānini manasy aṅgīkṛtā kalkitā  RUnm 
athavedaṃ priyoktitvāt sāmodāharaṇaṃ bhavet 
nāyakasya svavacasā bhaṅgyāyaṃ bheda īryate  RUnm 
yathā
rūkṣā yan mayi vartase tvam abhitaḥ snigdhe'pi te dūṣaṇaṃ
tatrāste na hi kintu tat kila mamānaucityajātaṃ phalam 
yena svastaruṇīr upekṣya caramām apy āśrayantīr daśāṃ
premārtaṃ vrajayauvataṃ ca sumukhi tvaṃ kevalaṃ sevyase  RUnm 
sakhyādibhir upālambhaprayogo yathā
kartuṃ sundari śaṅkhacūḍamathane nāsminn upekṣocitā
sarveṣām abhayapradānapadavībaddhavrate preyasi 
ity ālībhir alakṣitaṃ murabhidā bhadrāvalī bheditā
nāsāgre varamauktikaśriyam adhād asrasya sā bindunā  RUnm 
atha dānam
vyājena bhūṣaṇādīnāṃ pradānaṃ dānam ucyate  RUnm 
yathā
kāmo nāma suhṛn mamāsti bhavatīm ākarṇya matpreyasīṃ
hāras tena tavārpito'yam urasi prāpnotu saṅgotsavam 
ity unnamya karaṃ muradviṣi vadaty udbhinnasāndrasmitā
padmā mānavinigrahāt praṇayinā tenodbhaṭaṃ cumbitā  RUnm 
atha natiḥ
kevalaṃ dainyam ālambya pādapāto natir matā  RUnm 
yathā
kṣitiluṭhitaśikhaṇḍāpīḍam ārān mukunde
racayati ratikāntastomakānte praṇāmam 
nayanajaladharābhyāṃ kurvatī bāṣpavṛṣṭiṃ
varatanur iha mānagrīṣmanāśaṃ śaśaṃsa  RUnm 
atha upekṣā
sāmādau tu parikṣīṇe syād upekṣāvadhīraṇam 
upekṣā kathyate kaiścit tūṣṇīmbhāvatayā sthitiḥ  RUnm 
tad dvayaṃ yathā
sūnur vallabha eṣa vallavapates tatrāpi vīrāgraṇī
statrāpi smaramaṇḍalīvijayinā rūpeṇa vibhrājitaḥ 
sakhyaḥ samprati rūkṣatā pṛthur iyaṃ tenātra na śreyase
dūre paśyata yāti niṣṭhuramanāḥ kā yuktir atrocitā  RUnm 
māne muhur nitibhir apy atidurnivāre
vācaṃyamavratam ahaṃ tarasāgrahīṣam 
bāṣpaṃ tato vikiratī nijagāda padmā
pauṣpaṃ rajaḥ patitam atra dṛśor mameti  RUnm 
athavā
prasādanavidhiṃ muktvā vākyair anyārthasūcakaiḥ 
prasādanaṃ mṛgākṣīṇām upekṣeti smṛtā budhaiḥ  RUnm 
yathā
dhammille navamālatī paricitā savye ca śabdagrahe
mallī sundari dakṣiṇe tu katarat puṣpaṃ tava bhrājate 
āghreyaṃ paricetum ity upahite vyājena nāsāpuṭe
gaṇḍodyatpulakā vihasya hariṇā candrāvalī cumbitā  RUnm 
atha rasāntaram
ākasmikabhayādīnāṃ prastutiḥ syād rasāntaram 
yādṛcchikaṃ buddhipūrvam iti dvedhā tad ucyate  RUnm 
tatra yādṛcchikam
upasthitam akasmād yat tad yādṛcchikam ucyate  RUnm 
yathā
api gurubhir upāyair adya sāmādibhir yā
lavam api na mṛgākṣī mānamudrām abhāṅkṣīt 
harim iha parirebhe sā svayaṃgrāham agre
navajaladharanādair bhīṣitā paśya bhadrā  RUnm 
yathā vā
upāyeṣu vyarthonnatiṣu bata sāmādiṣu sakhe
sakhīnāṃ cāturye gatavati ca sadyaḥ śithilatām 
viśākhāyāḥ kopajvaraharaṇamantrapratinidhiṃ
sacītkāraṃ rūkṣasvanitam akarod ukṣadanujaḥ  RUnm 
atha buddhipūrvam
buddhipūrvaṃ tu kāntena pratyutpannadhiyā kṛtam  RUnm 
yathā
pāṇau pañcamukhena duṣṭakṛmiṇā daṣṭo'smi roṣād iti
vyājāt kūṇitalocanaṃ vrajapatau vyābhujya vaktraṃ sthite 
sadyaḥ projjhitaroṣavṛttir asakṛt kiṃ vṛttam ity ākulā
jalpantī smitabandhur āsyam amunā gāndharvikā cumbitā  RUnm 
yathā vā
nyastaṃ dāma kṛtāgasādya hariṇā dṛṣṭvā puro rādhayā
kṣiptenābhihataḥ sa tena kapaṭī duḥkhīva bhugnānanaḥ 
mīlann eva niṣedivān bhuvi tataḥ sadyas tayā vyagrayā
pāñibhyāṃ dhṛtakandharaḥ sthitamukho bimboṣṭham asyāḥ papau
deśakālabalenaiva muralīśravaṇena ca 
vināpy upāyaṃ māno'sau līyate vrajasubhruvām  RUnm 
tatra deśabalena yathā
alaṅkīrṇaṃ candrāvalir alighaṭājhaṅkṛtibharaiḥ
puro vṛndāraṇyaṃ kim api kalayantī kusumitam 
hariṃ ca smerāsyaṃ priyakatarumūle priyam itaḥ
skhalanmānā sakhyām adiśata satṛṣṇaṃ dṛśam asau  RUnm 
kālabalena yathā
śaradi madhuramūrtiḥ paśya kānticchaṭābhiḥ
snapayati ravikanyātīravanyāṃ sudhāṃśuḥ 
iti niśi niśamayya vyāhṛtiṃ dūtikāyāḥ
smitarucibhir atānīt tatra rādhā prasādam  RUnm 
muralīśabdena yathā
yadi roṣaṃ na hi muñcasi
na muñca mama devi nātra nirbandhaḥ 
phutkṛtividhūtamānaḥ
sa bhavatu vijayī harer veṇuḥ  RUnm 
yathā vā
mānasyopādhyāyi prasīda sakhi rundhi me śrutidvandvam 
ayam uccāṭanamantraṃ siddho veṇur vane paṭhati  RUnm 
tāratamyaṃ tu mānasya hetoḥ syāt tāratamyataḥ 
syāl laghur madhyamaś cāsau mahiṣṭhaś cety atas tridhā  RUnm 
susādhyaḥ syāl laghur māno yatnasādhyasya madhyamaḥ 
duḥsādhyaḥ syād upāyena mahiṣṭhaḥ preyasāpy ayam  RUnm 
kṛṣṇe roṣoktayas tāsāṃ vāmo durlīlaśekharaḥ 
kitavendro mahādhūrtaḥ kaṭhoro nirapatrapaḥ  RUnm 
atidurlalito gopībhujaṅgo ratahiṇḍakaḥ 
gopikādharmavidhvaṃsī gopasādhvīviḍambakaḥ  RUnm 
kāmukeśas tamisraughaḥ śyāmātmāmbarataskaraḥ 
govardhanataṭāraṇyabāṭapāṭaccarādayaḥ  RUnm 
iti mānaḥ 
atha premavaicittyam
priyasya sannikarṣe'pi premonmādabhramād bhavet 
yā viśleṣadhiyārtis tat premavaicittyam ucyate  RUnm 
yathā
ābhīrendrasute sphuraty api puras tīvrānurāgotthayā
viśleṣajvarasampadā vivaśadhīr atyantam udghūrṇitā 
kāntaṃ me sakhi darśayeti daśanair udgūrṇaśasyāṅkurā
rādhā hanta tathā vyaceṣṭate yataḥ kṛṣṇo'py abhūd vismitaḥ  RUnm 
yathā vā vidagdhamādhave 
samajani davād vitrastānāṃ kim ārtaravo gavāṃ
mayi kim abhavad vaiguṇyaṃ vā niraṅkuśam īkṣitam 
vyaraci nibhṛtaṃ kiṃ vāhūtiḥ kayācid abhīṣṭayā
yad iha sahasā mām atyākṣīd vane vanajekṣaṇaḥ  RUnm 
vilāsam anurāgas tu kutracit kam api vrajam 
pārśve santam api preṣṭhaṃ hāritaṃ kurute sphuṭam  RUnm 
suṣṭhūdāharatā paṭṭamahiṣīgītavibhramam 
spaṣṭaṃ muktāphale caitad vopadevena varṇitam  RUnm 
iti premavaicittyam
atha pravāsaḥ
pūrvasaṅgatayor yūnor bhaved deśāntarādibhiḥ 
vyavadhānaṃ tu yat prājñaiḥ sa pravāsa itīryate  RUnm 
tajjanyavipralambho'yaṃ pravāsatvena kathyate 
harṣagarvamadavrīḍā varjayitvā samīritāḥ  RUnm 
śṛṅgārayogyāḥ sarve'pi pravāse vyabhicāriṇaḥ 
sa dvidhā buddhipūrvaḥ syāt tathiavābuddhipūrvakaḥ  RUnm 
atra buddhipūrvaḥ
dūre kāryānurodhena gamaḥ syād buddhipūrvakaḥ 
kāryaṃ kṛṣṇasya kathitaṃ svabhaktaprīṇanādikam  RUnm 
kiñcid dūre sudūre ca gamanād apy ayaṃ dvidhā  RUnm 
tatra ādyaḥ
dṛṣṭiṃ nidhāya surabhīnikurambavīthyāṃ
kṛṣṇeti varṇayugalābhyasena rasajñām 
śuśrūṣaṇe muralinisvanitasya karṇau
cittaṃ mukhe tava nayaty ahar adya rādhā  RUnm 
atha dvitīyaḥ
bhāvī bhavaṃś ca bhūtaś ca tirvidhaḥ sa tu kīrtyate  RUnm 
tatra bhāvī
yathā uddhavasandeśe 
eṣa kṣattā vrajanarapateḥ ājñayā gokule asmin
bāle prāto nagaragataye ghoṣaṇāmātanoti 
duṣṭam bhūyaḥ sphurati ca balādīkṣaṇaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ me
tena svāntaṃ sphuṭati caṭulam hanta bhāvyaṃ na jāne  RUnm 
bhavan yathā lalitamādhave 
bhānor bimbe tvaritam udayaprasthataḥ prasthite'sau
yātrānandīṃ paṭhati muditaḥ syandane gāndineyaḥ 
tāvat tūrṇaṃ sphuṭa khurapuṭaiḥ kṣauṇipṛṣṭaṃ khananto
yāvan nāmī hṛdaya bhavato ghoṭakāḥ sphoṭakā syuḥ  RUnm 
bhūto yathā uddhavasandeśe 
kāmaṃ dūre sahacari varīvarti yat kaṃsavairī
na idam lokottaramapi vipaddurdinaṃ me dunoti 
āśākīlo hṛdi kila vṛtaḥ prāṇarodhī tu yo me
so'yaṃ pīḍāṃ niviḍavaḍavāvahnitīvrastanoti  RUnm 
atra śrīyadusiṃhena preyasīhir amuṣya ca 
preṣaṇaṃ kriyate premṇā sandeśasya parasparam  RUnm 
yathā uddhavasandeśe 
soḍhavyaṃ te kathamapi balāccakṣuṣī mudrayitvā
tīvrottāpam hatamanasijoddāmavikrāntacakram 
dvitraireva priyasakhi dinaiḥ sevyatāṃ devi śavye
yāsyāmi tvatpraṇayacaṭulabhrūyugāḍambarāṇām  RUnm 
tathā padyāvalyām 
kālindyāḥ pulinaṃ pradoṣamaruto ramyāḥ śaśaṅkāṃśavaḥ
santāpaṃ na harantu nāma nitarāṃ kurvanti kasmāt punaḥ 
sandiṣṭaṃ vrajayoṣitām iti hareḥ saṃśṛṇvato'ntaḥpure
niḥśvāsāḥ prasṛtā jayanti ramaṇīsaubhāgyagarvacchidaḥ  RUnm 
atha abuddhipūrvaḥ
pāratntryodbhavo yas tu proktaḥ so'buddhipūrvakaḥ 
divyādivyādijanitaṃ pāratantryam anekadhā  RUnm 
yathā lalitamādhave 
ānītāsi mayā manorathaśatavyagreṇa nirbandhataḥ
pūrṇaṃ śāradapurṇimāparimalair vṛndāṭavīmaṇḍalam 
sadyaḥ sundari śaṅkhacūḍakapaṭaprāptodayenādhunā
daivenādya virodhinā katham itas tvaṃ hanta dūrīkṛtā  RUnm 
cintātra jāgarodvegau tānavaṃ malināṅgatā 
pralāpo vyādhir unmādo moho mṛtyur daśā daśa  RUnm 
tatra cintā
yathā haṃsadūte 
yadā yāto gopīhṛdayamadano nandasadanān
mukundo gāndinyāstanayamanuvindan madhupurīm 
tadāmānkṣīccintāsariti ghanaghūrṇāparicayair
agādhāyāṃ bādhāmayapayasi rādhā virahiṇī  RUnm 
atha jāgaraḥ
yathā padyāvalyāṃ 
yāḥ paśyanti priyaṃ svapne dhanyāstāḥ sakhi yoṣitaḥ 
asmākaṃ tu gate kṛṣṇe gatā nidrāpi vairiṇī  RUnm 
atha udvegaḥ
yathā haṃsadūte 
mano me hā kaṣṭaṃ jvalati kimahaṃ hanta karavai
na pāraṃ nāvāraṃ kimapi kalayāmy asya jaladheḥ 
iyaṃ vande mūrdhnā sapadi tamupāyaṃ kathaya māṃ
parāmṛṣye yasmāddhṛtikaṇikayāpe kṣaṇikayā  RUnm 
atha tānavaṃ yathā
udañcadvaktrāmbhoruhavikṛtir antaḥkaluṣitā
sadāhārābhāvaglapitakucakokā yadupate 
viśuṣyantī rādhā tava virahatāpād anudinaṃ
nidāghe kulyeva kraśimaparipākaṃ prathayati  RUnm 
atha malināṅgatā
himavisaraviśīrṇāmbhojatulyānanaśrīḥ
kharamarudaparajyadbandhujīvopamauṣṭhī 
aghahara śaradarkottāpitendīvarākṣī
tava virahavipattimlāpitāsīd viśākhā  RUnm 
atha pralāpaḥ
yathā lalitamādhave 
kva nandakulacandramāḥ kva śikhicandrakālaṅkṛtiḥ
kva mandramuralīravaḥ kva nu surendranīladyutiḥ
kva rāsarasatāṇḍavī kva sakhi jīvarakṣauṣadhir
nidhir mama suhṛttamaḥ kva bata hanta hā dhigvidhim  RUnm 
atha vyādhiḥ
yathā tatraiva 
uttāpī puṭapākato pi garalagrāmād api kṣobhaṇo
dambholer api duḥsahaḥ kaṭur alaṃ hṛnmagnaśūlyād api
tīvraḥ prauḍhavisūcikānicayato py uccair mamāyaṃ balī
marmāṇy adya bhinatti gokulapater viśleṣajanmā jvaraḥ  RUnm 
atha unmādaḥ
bhramati bhavanagarbhe nirnimittaṃ hasantī
prathayati tava vārtāṃ cetanācetaneṣu 
lutḥati ca bhuvi rādhā kampitāṅgī murāre
viṣamavirahakhedodgārivibhrāntacittā  RUnm 
yathā vā
adyākāṇḍikam aṭṭahāsapaṭalaṃ nirmāti gharmāmbubhāk
cītkāraṃ kurute camatkṛtiparā sotkaṇṭham ākasmikam 
ākrandaṃ vitanoti ghargharaghanodghoṣaṃ kilātarkitaṃ
rādhā mādhavaviprayogarabhasād anyeva tīvrād abhūt  RUnm 
atha mohaḥ
nirundhe dainyābdhiṃ harati gurucintā paribhavaṃ
vilumpaty unmādaṃ sthagayati balād bāṣpalaharīm 
idānīṃ kaṃsāre kuvalayadṛśaḥ kevalam idaṃ
vidhatte sācivyaṃ tava virahamūrcchāsahacarī  RUnm 
atha mṛtyuḥ
yathā haṃsadūte 
aye rāsakrīḍārasika mama sakhyāṃ navanavā
purā baddhā yena praṇayalaharī hanta gahanā 
sa cen muktāpekṣastvamapi dhig imāṃ tulaśakalaṃ
yadetasyā nāsānihitamidamadyāpi calati  RUnm 
pravāsavipralambhe'smin daśās tās tā harer api 
atropalakṣaṇāyaikam udāharaṇam īryate  RUnm 
yathā
krīḍāratnagṛhe viḍambitapayaḥphenāvalīmārdane
talpe necchati kalpaśākhicamarīramye'pi rājñāṃ sutāḥ 
kintu dvāravatīpatir vrajagiridroṇīvilāntaḥśilā
paryaṅkopari rādhikāratikalāṃ dhyāyan muhuḥ klāmyati  RUnm 
proktānāṃ premabhedānāṃ vividhatvād daśā api 
vividhāḥ syur ihety etā bhūmabhītyā na kīrtitāḥ  RUnm 
etās tu premabhedānām anubhāvatayā daśāḥ 
sādhāraṇyaḥ samastānāṃ prāyaśaḥ sambhavanty api  RUnm 
kintv atraivādhirūḍhasya mohanatvam apeyuṣaḥ 
asādhāraṇarūpās tu tatprasaṅge puroditāḥ  RUnm 
vipralambhaṃ paraṃ kecit karuṇābhidham ucire 
sa pravāsaviśeṣatvān naivātra pṛthag īritaḥ  RUnm 
iti vipralambhabhedāḥ
atha saṃyogaviyogasthitiḥ
harer līlāviśeṣasya prakaṭasyānusārataḥ 
varṇitā virahāvasthā goṣṭhavāmabhruvām asau  RUnm 
vṛndāraṇye viharatā sadā rāsādivibhramaiḥ 
hariṇā vrajadevīnāṃ viraho'sti na karhicit  RUnm 
tathā ca pādme pātālakhaṇḍe mathurāmāhātmye
gogopagopikāsaṅge yatra krīḍati kaṃsahā  RUnm 
iti 
iti saṃyogaviyogasthitiḥ
atha sambhogaḥ
darśanāliṅganādīnāṃ ānukūlyān niṣevayā 
yūnor ullāsam ārohan bhāvaḥ sambhoga ucyate  RUnm 
manīṣibhir ayaṃ mukho gauṇaś ceti dvidhoditaḥ  RUnm 
tatra mukhyaḥ
mukhyo jāgradavasthāyāṃ sambhogaḥ sa caturvidhaḥ  RUnm 
tān pūrvarāgato mānāt pravāsadvayataḥ kramāt 
jātān saṃkṣiptasaṅkīrṇasampannarddhimato viduḥ  RUnm 
tatra saṅkṣiptaḥ
yuvānau yatra saṃkṣiptān sādhvasavrīḍitādibhiḥ 
upacārān niṣevete sa saṃkṣipta itīritaḥ  RUnm 
tatra nāyakena kṛtaḥ
yathā saptaśatyām
līlāhituliaselo rakkhau vo rāhiātthaṇapphaṃse 
hariṇo paḍhamasamāgamasajjhasabebellio hattho  RUnm 
līlābhitulitaśailo rakṣatu vo rādhikāstanasparśe 
hareḥ prathamasamāgamasādhvasavevellito hastaḥ 
nāyikāyāḥ yathā
cumbe paṭāvṛtamukhī navasaṅgame'bhū
dāliṅgane kuṭilitāṅgalatā tadāsīt 
avyaktavāg ajani kelikathāsu rādhā
modaṃ tathāpi vidadhe madhusūdanasya  RUnm 
atha saṅkīrṇaḥ
yatra saṅkīryamāṇāḥ syur vyalīkasmaraṇādibhiḥ 
upacārāḥ sa saṅkīrṇaḥ kiñcit taptekṣupeśalaḥ  RUnm 
yathā
sāsūyajalpitasudhāni samatsarāṇi
manoparāmaramaṇīyadṛgiṅgitāni 
kaṃsadviṣaḥ sphuradamandamukhāny anaṅga
vikrīḍitāni saha rādhikayā jayanti  RUnm 
yathā vā
vaktraṃ kiñcid avāñcitaṃ vivṛṇute nātiprasādodayaṃ
dṛṣṭir bhugnataṭā vyanakti śanakair īrṣyāvaśeṣacchaṭām 
rādhāyāḥ sakhi sūcayaty aviśadā vāg apy asūyākalāṃ
mānantaṃ bruvatī tathāpi madhurā kṛṣṇaṃ dhinoty ākṛtiḥ  RUnm 
atha sampannaḥ
pravāsāt saṅgate kānte bhogaḥ sampanna īritaḥ 
dvidhā syād āgatiḥ prādurbhāvaś ceti sa saṅgamaḥ  RUnm 
tatra āgatiḥ
laukikavyavahāreṇa syād āgamanam āgatiḥ  RUnm 
yathā uddhavasandeśe 
mā mandākṣaṃ kuru gurujanāddehalīṃ gehamadhyā
dehi klāntā divasamakhilam hanta viśleṣato'si 
eṣa smero milati mṛdule vallavīcittahārī
hārī guñjāvalibhiralibhirlīḍhagandho mukundaḥ  RUnm 
atha prādurbhāvaḥ
preṣṭhānāṃ premasaṃrambhavihvalānāṃ puro hariḥ 
āvirbhavaty akasmād yat prādurbhāvaḥ sa ucyate  RUnm 
yathā śrīdaśame 
tāsām āvirabhūc chauriḥ smayamānamukhāmbujaḥ 
pītāmbaradharaḥ sragvī sākṣān manmathamanmathaḥ  RUnm 
yathā vā haṃsadūte 
ayi svapno dūre viramatu samakṣaṃ śṛṇu haṭhā
daviśvastā mā bhūriha sakhi manovibhramadhiyā 
vayasyaste govardhanavipinamāsādya kutukā
dakāṇḍe yadbhūyaḥ smarakalahapāṇḍityamatanot  RUnm 
rūḍhākhyabhāvajāto'yaṃ sambhogo vaipralambhikaḥ 
nirbharānandapurāṇāṃ paramāvadhir iṣyate  RUnm 
dviguṇā virahārtiḥ syāt sphuraṇe veṇurāgaje 
prādurbhāve bhavaty atra sarvābhīṣṭasukhotsavaḥ  RUnm 
atha samṛddhimān
durlabhālokayor yūnoḥ pāratantryād viyuktayoḥ 
upabhogātireko yaḥ kīrtyate sa samṛddhimān  RUnm 
yathā lalitamādhave 
dagdhaṃ hanta dadhānayā vapur idaṃ yasyāvalokāśayā
soḍhā marmavipāṭane paṭur iyaṃ pīḍātivṛṣṭir mayā 
kālindīyataṭīkuṭīrakuharakrīḍābhisāravratī
so'yaṃ jīvitabandhur induvadane bhūyaḥ samāliṅgitaḥ  RUnm 
yathā vā 
tavātra parimṛgyatā kim api lakṣma sākṣād iyaṃ
mayā tvam upasāditā nikhilalokalakṣmīr asi 
yathā jagati cañcatā caṇakamuṣṭisampattaye
janena patitā puraḥ kanakavṛṣṭir āsādyate  RUnm 
iti madhurarasaparipākavivekaḥ 
atha gauṇasambhogaḥ
channaprakāśabhedena kaiścid eṣāṃ dvirūpatā 
iṣṭāpy atra na hi proktā nātyullāsakarī yataḥ  RUnm 
atha gauṇaḥ
svapne prāptiviśeṣo'sya harer gauṇa itīryate 
svapno dvidhātra sāmānyaviśeṣatvena kīrtitaḥ  RUnm 
sāmānyaḥ sa tu yaḥ pūrvaṃ kathito vyabhicāriṣu 
viśeṣaḥ khalu jāgaryā nirviśeṣao mahādbhutaḥ  RUnm 
bhāvautkaṇṭhyemayo hy eṣa caturdhā pūrvavan mataḥ  RUnm 
tatra svapne saṅkṣipto yathā
vihāraṃ kurvāṇas taraṇitanayātīravipine
navāmbhodaśreṇīmadhurimaviḍambidyutibharaḥ 
vidagdhānāṃ cūḍāmaṇir anudinaṃ cumbati mukhaṃ
mama svapne ko'pi priyasakhi balīyān navayuvā  RUnm 
atha svapne saṅkīrṇo yathā
sakhi kruddhā mā bhūr laghur api na doṣaḥ sumukhi me
na mānāgnijvālām aśamayam ahaṃ tām asamaye 
sa dhūrtas te svapne rasavṛṣṭiṃ mayi tathā
yato vistīrṇāpi svayam iyam ayāsīd upaśamam  RUnm 
atha svapne sampannaḥ
yathā haṃsadūte 
prayāto māṃ hitvā yadi kaṭhinacūḍāmaṇirasau
paryātu svacchandaṃ mama samayadharmaḥ kila gatiḥ 
idaṃ soḍhuṃ kā vā prabhavati yataḥ svapnakapaṭā
dihāyāto vṛndāvanabhuvi kalān māṃ ramayati  RUnm 
atha svāpnasamṛddhimān
yathā lalitamādhave 
cirād adya svapne mama vividhayatnād upagate
prapede govindaḥ sakhi nayanayor akṣaṇabhuvam 
gṛhītvā hā hanta tvaritam atha tasminn api rathaṃ
kathaṃ pratyāsannaḥ sa khalu puruṣo rājapuruṣaḥ  RUnm 
tulyasvarūpa evāyaṃ prodyan yūnor dvayor api 
ūṣāniruddhayor yadvat kvacit svapno'py abādhitaḥ  RUnm 
ataeva hi siddhānāṃ svapne'pi paramādbhute 
prāptāni maṇḍanādīni dṛśyante jāgare'pi ca  RUnm 
vyatītya turyām api saṃśritānāṃ
tāṃ pañcamīṃ premamayīm avasthām 
na sambhavaty eva haripriyāṇāṃ
svapno rajovṛttivijṛmbhito yaḥ  RUnm 
ity eṣa haribhāvasya vilāsaḥ ko'pi peśala 
citrasvapnam ivātanvan kṛṣṇaḥ saṅgamayaty alam  RUnm 
athaiteṣu nirūpyante tadviśeṣāḥ supeśalāḥ 
ye'nubhāvadaśām asyāḥ prāpnuvanti rateḥ sphuṭam  RUnm 
te tu sandarśanaṃ jalpaḥ sparśanaṃ vartmarodhanam 
rāsavṛndāvankrīḍāyamunādyambukelayaḥ  RUnm 
naukhelā līlayā cauryaṃ ghaṭṭaḥ kuñjādilīnatā 
madhupānaṃ vadhūveśadhṛtiḥ kapaṭasuptatā  RUnm 
dyūtakrīḍā paṭākṛṣṭiś cumbāśleṣau nakhārpaṇam 
bimbādharasudhāpānaḥ samprayogādayo matāḥ  RUnm 
tatra sandarśanaṃ
yathā lalitamādhave 
calākṣigurulokataḥ sphurati tāvad antarbhayaṃ
kulasthitir alaṃ tu me manasi tāvad unmīlati 
calanmakarakuṇḍalasphuritaphullagaṇḍasthalaṃ
na yāvad aparokṣatām idam apaiti vaktrāmbujam  RUnm 
atha jalpaḥ
jalpaḥ parasparaṃ goṣṭhī vitathoktiś ca kathyate  RUnm 
atra parasparaḥ goṣṭhī
yathā dānakelikaumudyām 
dharṣaṇe nakulastrīṇāṃ bhujaṅgeśaḥ kṣamaḥ katham 
yad etā daśanair eṣa daśan nāpnoti maṅgalam  RUnm 
aprauḍhadvijarājarājadalikā labdhā vibhūtiṃ rucāṃ
navyām ātmani kṛṣṇavartmavilasaddṛṣṭir viśākhāñcitā 
kandarpasya vidagdhatāṃ vidadhatI netrāñcalasya tviṣā
tvaṃ rādhe śivamūrtir ity urasi māṃ bhogīndram aṅgīkuru  RUnm 
vitathoktiḥ
yathā tatraiva 
asminn adrau kati na hi mayā hanta hārādivittaṃ
hāraṃ hāraṃ hariṇanayanā grāhitā jainadīkṣām 
yāḥ kākūktisthagitavadanāḥ patradānena dīnās
tūrṇaṃ dūrād anujagṛhire prauḍhavallīsakhībhiḥ  RUnm 
atha sparśanam yathā
na kuru śapatham asya sparśato dūṣitoccair
asi bhujabhujagena tvaṃ bhujaṅgādhipasya 
tanur anupamakampā svedam abhyudgirantī
kapaṭini paritas te paśya romāñcitāsti  RUnm 
atha vartmarodhanaṃ
yathā vidagdhamādhave 
parītaṃ śṛṅgeṇa sphuṭataraśilāśyāmalarucaṃ
valadvetraṃ vaṃśavyatikaralasanmekhalam amum 
atikramyottuṅgaṃ dharaṇidharam agre katham itas
tvayā gantuṃ śakyā taraṇiduhitus tīrasaraṇī  RUnm 
atha rāso yathā
harir navaghanākṛtiḥ prativadhūdvayaṃ madhyatas
tadaṃsavilasadbhujo bhramati citram eko'py asau 
vadhūś ca taḍidujjvalā pratiharid vayaṃ madhyataḥ
sakhīdhṛtakarāmbujā naṭati paśya rāsotsave  RUnm 
atha vṛndāvanakrīḍā
sthalakamalamalīnāṃ stauti gītaiḥ padaṃ te
radatatimatinamrā vandate kundarājī 
adharam anubhajantī lambate bimbamālā
vilasati tava vaśyā paśya vṛndāṭavīyam  RUnm 
yamunājalakeliḥ yathā
vyātyukṣīyudhi rādhayā ghanarasaiḥ paryukṣyamāṇasya te
mālyaṃ bhaṅgam avāpa vīra tilako yātaḥ kilādṛśyatām 
vaktrendau pratimācchalena śaraṇaṃ labdhaḥ sakhīṃ kaustubhas
tan mā bhūś cakito vimuktacikuraṃ nārdaty asau tvadvidham  RUnm 
yathā vā padyāvalyāṃ 
jalakelitaralakaratala
muktapunaḥpihitarādhikāvadanaḥ 
jagad avatu kokayūnor
vighaṭanasaṅghaṭanakautukī kṛṣṇaḥ  RUnm 
atha naukhelā
yathā padyāvalyāṃ 
muktā taraṅganivahena pataṅgaputrī
navyā ca naur iti vacas tava tathyam eva 
śaṅkānidānam idam eva mamātimātraṃ
tvaṃ cañcalo yad iha mādhava nāviko'si  RUnm 
atha līlācauryam
līlācauryaṃ bhaved vaṃśīvastrapuṣpādihāritā  RUnm 
atha vaṃśīcauryam
yathā padyāvalyāṃ 
nīcair nyāsād atha caraṇayor nūpura mūkayantī
dhṛtvā dhṛtvā katakavalayāny utkṣipantī bhujānte 
mudrām akṣṇoś cakitaṃ śaśvad ālokayantī
smitvā smitvā harati muralīm aṅkato mādhavasya  RUnm 
atha vastracauryaṃ yathā
chadāvalivṛtaiva naḥ sapadi kācid ekā vrajaṃ
praviśya jaratīr ihānayatu ghorakarmoddhatāḥ 
ayaṃ guṇanidhis taror upari tābhir abhyarcyatām
umāvratakumārikāpaṭalacelapāṭaccaraḥ  RUnm 
atha puṣpacauryaṃ yathā
ayi jñātaṃ jñātaṃ harasi hariṇākṣi pratidinaṃ
tvam eva pracchannā mama sumanasāṃ mañjarim itaḥ 
cirād diṣṭyā cauri tvam iha vidhṛtādya svayam ato
guhākārām ārāt praviśa vasatiṃ prauḍhibhir alam  RUnm 
atha ghaṭṭaḥ
yathā dānakelikaumudyām 
ghaṭṭādhirājam avamatya vivādam eva
yūyaṃ yad ācaratha śulkam adityamānāḥ 
manye vidhitsatha tad atra gires taṭeṣu
durgeṣu hanta viṣameṣu raṇābhiyogam  RUnm 
atha kuñjādilīnatā
yathā vidagdhamādhave 
śaṅke saṅkulitāntarādya niviḍakrīḍānubandhecchayā
kuñje vañjulaśākhinaḥ śaśimukhī līnā varīvarti sā 
no ced eṣa tadaṅghrisaṅgamavinābhāvād akāle kathaṃ
puṣpāmodanimantritālipaṭalīstotrasya pātrībhavet  RUnm 
atha madhupānaṃ yathā
mukhavidhum uditaṃ madhudviṣo'sau
madhucaṣake madhuraṃ samīkṣya mugdhā 
adiśata dṛśam eva tatra pātuṃ
na tu vadanaṃ muhur arthitāpi tena  RUnm 
atha vadhūveśadhṛtiḥ
yathā uddhavasandeśe 
keyaṃ śyāmā sphurati sarale gopakanyā kimarthaṃ
prāptā sakhyaṃ tava mṛgayate nirmitāsau vayasyā 
āliṅgāmūṃ muhuriti tathā kurvatī māṃ viditvā
nārīveśam hriyamupayayau māninī yatra rādhā  RUnm 
kapaṭasuptatā
yathā karṇāmṛte 
stokastokanirudhyamānamṛdulaprasyandimandasmitaṃ
premodbhedanirargalaprasṛmarapravyaktaromodgamam 
śrotuṃ śrotramanoharaṃ vrajavadhūlīlāmitho jalpitaṃ
mithyāsvāpam upāsmahe bhagavataḥ krīḍānimīladdṛśaḥ  RUnm 
atha dyūtakrīḍā
jitvā dyūtapaṇaṃ daśaty aghahare gaṇḍaṃ mudā dakṣiṇaṃ
sā vāmaṃ ca daśeti tatra rabhasād akṣaṃ kṣipanty abhyadhāt 
ājñāṃ sundari te yatheti hariṇā vāme ca daṣṭe tataḥ
saṃrambhād iva sā bhujālatikayā kaṇṭhe babandha priyam  RUnm 
atha paṭṭākṛṣṭiḥ
yathā lalitamādhave 
dhanyaḥ so'yaṃ maṇir aviraladhvāntapuñje nikuñje
smitvā smitvā mayi kucapaṭīṃ kṛṣṭavaty unmadena 
gāḍhaṃ gūḍhākṛtir api tayā manmukhākutavedī
niṣṭhīvan yaḥ kiraṇalaharīṃ hrepayāmāsa rādhām  RUnm 
atha cumbo yathā
kapaṭacaṭulitabhruvaḥ samantā
nmukhaśaśinaḥ rabhasād vidhūyamānam 
danujaripur acumbad ambujākṣyāḥ
kamalam ivānilakampi cañcarīkaḥ  RUnm 
atha āśleṣo yathā
navajāguḍavarṇayopagūḍhaḥ
sphuradabhradyutir etayonmadena 
harati sma harir hiraṇyavallī
parivītāṅgatamālamaṅgalāni  RUnm 
atha nakhakṣataṃ yathā
na kucāv imau gatijitā tayā hṛtaṃ
gajataḥ prasahya sakhi kumbhayor yugam 
kṣatam atra nāgadamano yad arpaya
tparamaṅgajāṅkuśavareṇa tatkṣaṇam  RUnm 
atha bimbādharasudhāpānaṃ yathā
na hi sudhākarabimbasudhākaraṃ
kuru mukhaṃ karabhoru karāvṛtam 
adhararaṅgaṇam aṅga varāṅgane
pibatu nīpavanībhramaras tava  RUnm 
atha samprayogo yathā
drāgdormaṇḍalapīḍanoddhuradhiyaḥ proddāmavaijātyayā
nirbandhād adharāmṛtāni pibataḥ sītkārapūrṇāsyayā 
kandarpotsavapaṇḍitasya maṇiatir ākrāntakuñjāntayā
sārdhaṃ rādhikayā harer nidhuvanakrīḍāvidhir vardhate  RUnm 
vidagdhānāṃ mitho līlāvilāsena yathā sukham 
na tathā samprayogeṇa syād evaṃ rasikā viduḥ  RUnm 
yathā
balena parirambhaṇe nakhaśikhābhir ullekhanaṃ
haṭhād adharakhaṇḍane bhujayugena bandhakriyām 
dukūladalane hatiḥ kuvalayena kurvāṇayā
ratād api sukhaṃ harer adhikam ādadhe rādhayā  RUnm 
yathā vā
narmotsekakalādṛgañcalacamatkārī bhruvor vibhramaḥ
saṃvyānasya vikarṣaṇ caṭulatāṃ karṇotpalenāhatiḥ 
krīḍeyaṃ vrajanāgarīratiguror gāndharvikāyās tathā
bhūyiṣṭhaṃ suratotsavād api navāsvādaṃ vitene sukham  RUnm 
ataeva śrīgītagovinde 
pratyūhapulakāṅkureṇa niviḍaleśanimeṣeṇa ca
krīḍākūtavilokite'dharasudhāpāne kathākelibhiḥ 
ānandādhigamena manmathakalāyuddhe'pi yasminn abhud
udbhūtaḥ sa tayor babhūva suratārambhaḥ priyambhāvukaḥ  RUnm 
yathā
gokulānanda govinda goṣṭhendrakulacandramaḥ 
prāṇeśa sundarottaṃsa nāgarāṇāṃ śikhāmaṇeḥ  RUnm 
vṛndāvanavidho goṣṭhayuvarāja manohara 
ity ādyā vrajadevīnāṃ preyasī praṇayoktayaḥ  RUnm 
atulatvād apāratvād āpto'sau durvigāhatām 
spṛṣṭaḥ paraṃ taṭasthena rasābdhir madhuro mayā o
ayam ujjvalanīlamaṇir gahanamahāghoṣasāgaraprabhavaḥ 
bhajatu tava makarakuṇḍalaparisarasevaucitīṃ deva o
iti sambhogabhedāḥ 
iti śrīśrīujjvalanīlamaṇau śṛṅgārabhedaprakaraṇam 
sampūrṇo'yaṃ śrīśrīlarūpagosvāmi
prabhupādapraṇītaśrīśrīujjvalanīlamaṇir nāma granthaḥ
